Rome and Tokyo Officially Announce; Italy and Japan Establish Agreement; Confirming Japan's Economic Rights and Interests in Abyssinia; Italy to Establish Consulate in Manchuria 52

(Tokyo) Regarding the respect for Japan's vested interests in Abyssinia and the understanding between Japan and Italy on the establishment of consulates, the Japanese Foreign Ministry, after consultation with the Italian government, issued the following statement at 8:00 PM on the 2nd (noon Rome time):

The Government of the Empire of Japan hereby informs the Italian Government of its intention to close its embassy in Abyssinia and to open a consulate in Addis Ababa. The Italian Government respects the Empire's trade and other interests in Abyssinia and will give them favorable consideration. (Domei News Agency, 2nd)

(Tokyo) The Foreign Ministry issued a statement on the evening of the 2nd, stating that the Japanese government has notified the Italian government that Japan is preparing to close its embassy in Abyssinia and to establish a consulate in Addis Ababa. The Italian government has also agreed to respect Japan's commercial and other interests in Abyssinia and to give them special consideration. The above announcement intentionally avoids mentioning the agreement between Italy and "Manchuria" regarding the establishment of an Italian consulate-general in Shenyang, but it is issued simultaneously in a separate written statement, stating that this matter has nothing to do with Japan's establishment of a consulate in Abyssinia. One of the most noteworthy points in this statement is that although there are currently no political negotiations underway, it is a well-known fact that Japan and Italy are working to cultivate friendly relations between the two countries through cooperation in culture and other fields. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

(Rome) Regarding Japan's recognition of the Italian Empire and Italy's de facto recognition of "Manchukuo," after the two sides agreed to issue separate announcements, the Italian government issued the first announcement today, stating that "Japanese Ambassador Sugimura recently met with Foreign Minister Ciano and informed him that the government wished to change the embassy in Addis Ababa into a consulate-general and requested King Victor Emmanuel III, also Emperor of Abyssinia, to issue the necessary consular credentials. Foreign Minister Ciano expressed his gratitude for this move by the Japanese Imperial Government and assured Ambassador Sugimura that the Italian authorities would pay special attention to the interests held by Japan in Abyssinia. The second announcement, which announces the establishment of an Italian consulate-general in Changchun, the capital of 'Manchukuo,' will not be issued until a week later." (Havas News Agency, 2nd)

Japanese Statement; Solely of an Economic Nature 53

(Tokyo) The Japanese Foreign Ministry issued a statement at 8:00 PM on the 2nd, along with the following remarks: "Considering the changing situation in Abyssinia and the timing thereof, we deem it appropriate to abolish the Imperial Embassy in Abyssinia and establish a consulate. Therefore, at the end of June this year, we instructed our ambassadors in Europe to pay attention to the situation in Abyssinia and the movements of member states of the League of Nations. As a result of negotiations with the Italian government, this has now come to fruition. The German government notified the Italian government on July 25 of this year that it would abolish its embassy in Abyssinia and establish a consulate-general, etc., and this was announced at the time. The Imperial Government's decision to establish a consulate this time, with the Italian government stating that it would give favorable consideration to the protection of commerce and other interests, is based on that statement. In order to adjust trade relations between Japan and Abyssinia, we expect to begin discussions. Apart from this, there are currently no political agreements being discussed between Japan and Italy. However, it is well known that the two countries are cultivating amicable relations through cultural exchange, etc. Furthermore, the Italian government and the government of 'Manchukuo' have been in consultation regarding the establishment of an Italian consulate in Shenyang, which is separate and unrelated to the establishment of a consulate in Abyssinia. This is added to avoid any misunderstanding." (Domei News Agency, 2nd)

(Tokyo) Since the conclusion of the agreement between Italy and Japan, Japan's commercial rights and interests in Abyssinia have been confirmed in principle. Therefore, Foreign Minister Arita will continue negotiations in Rome based on this general outline, and will proceed to conclude a commercial treaty based on this principle. The form of the agreement will be realized by an exchange of notes, but whether the procedure adopted will be to expand the area of application of the existing Italian-Japanese commercial treaty or to conclude a separate exchange of notes has not yet been decided. However, in preparation for the future economic development of Abyssinia, measures will be taken to ensure the promotion of Japanese commercial rights and interests. Currently, Japan's trade relations with Abyssinia are unclear due to the incompleteness of Abyssinian trade statistics, but if we combine imports through French Djibouti and through Indian merchants, rough goods such as coarse cloth are estimated at 10 million yuan. Therefore, ensuring this export volume will have an effect on trade. On the other hand, imports from Abyssinia are currently virtually nonexistent, and the region is very suitable for cotton cultivation. The Italian government is also gradually developing it according to plan. Therefore, the issue of securing cotton and other economic resources will also be included in the negotiations when concluding a commercial treaty in the future. As for the fact that Italy has newly established a consulate-general in Shenyang, and that Italy and "Manchukuo" will have a closer tendency, it is expected that this will have a positive impact on its commerce. (Domei News Agency, 2nd)

Rome's Explanation; Using This to Connect East and West 54

(Rome) Regarding the agreement established between Italy and Japan, government officials recently declared that since Japan maintains important interests in East Africa, Italy and Japan have established an agreement of a commercial nature. Observers say that Italy had felt uneasy about the importance of Japan's interests in Abyssinia, which can be seen from Italy's protest when Abyssinia was not yet destroyed and it repeatedly granted privileges to Japan. As for what commercial interests Italy maintains in "Manchukuo," no opinion is expressed. Political observers say that although newspapers in various countries have expressed opposition since 1934 to the fact that Japanese goods are flooding European markets, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has not been moved. The agreement established between Italy and Japan this time is in line with this aim, because the Prime Minister has always advocated attaching importance to countries in the East that are progressing, and wants to use Italy as a medium to connect East and West. It is also remembered that when students from various Asian countries held a conference in Rome in 1933, the Prime Minister attended and gave a speech, saying, "Europe is no longer in a leading position among the continents. It can still save itself in the future, but it must find a reasonable way so that all countries in the world can understand each other." In addition, political figures also declared that Japanese Ambassador Sugimura contributed a great deal to the establishment of the agreement between Italy and Japan, and that he also advised his own government when Italy conquered Abyssinia, which was successful. (Havas News Agency, 2nd)

Soviet Congress; Passes New Draft Constitution; Elects 220 People; To Form a Compilation and Review Committee 58

(Moscow) The draft of the new Soviet Constitution, drafted by Stalin a few months ago, was unanimously passed today at the All-Union Congress amid cheers of "Long Live Stalin." A committee of 220 people has now been elected, chaired by Stalin, to compile the final draft, which will include the amendments passed by the Central Executive Committee. The new constitution stipulates democratic elections and party rule, and stipulates the establishment of a President and a Senate and House of Representatives, all three of which are elected by direct secret ballot. The voting rights of farmers and workers in towns and cities are equal. The Constitution will recognize work as a fundamental right of citizens, and will recognize civil rights and property rights. The Senate will have 200 senators, and the House of Representatives will have 600 representatives. (Reuters, 2nd)

Although the matters to be debated will be limited to those included in the agenda, the former proposal may be discussed. The conference is expected to last until Christmas. (Reuters, 1st)

Buenos Aires, Argentina - The Pan-American Peace Conference opened here today. U.S. President Roosevelt delivered the opening address as follows: "The countries of the Americas have thoroughly discussed the psychology of modern warfare. Mr. Roosevelt strongly criticized certain world forces, without explicitly naming them, and said that the civilians of the world all want to live their lives in peace. All those who are militaristic and aggressive are only their leaders and governments. Moreover, such foolish countries will inevitably use their destructive weapons to attack their neighbors, or fall into total collapse due to the country's economic exhaustion. When these two situations occur, even if the countries of the Americas are not drawn into the vortex of war, they will inevitably be affected. It should be known that when a great war occurs elsewhere, our happiness will be affected everywhere. Therefore, the republics of the Americas should assist the countries of the Old World in avoiding war. I am confident that this can be done.

First, we must prevent the countries of the Americas from fighting among themselves. The best way to do this is to consolidate the constitutional democratic political system. In this way, we can distinguish ourselves from the people under other political systems and strive to maintain a peaceful life. At the same time, we must cooperate closely so that when other countries driven mad by war try to invade us, they will discover that the countries of the Americas are prepared and ready to discuss and protect their security together. What concerns us most at present is any country that lacks social and political equality.

Mr. Roosevelt also strongly condemned the harm of trade barriers, saying that those countries that are trying their best to promote these methods are often those who advocate war as an instrument of policy. The modern countries that are superstitious about the theory of self-sufficiency often cause the intellectual standards of their people to decline, the concept of democracy to be lost, and their efforts to increase armaments to double. Due to the above-mentioned suicidal policies and the suffering they cause, most of their people, in despair, generate the negative idea that the cost of war is lower than the cost of peace."

Mr. Roosevelt continued, "The realization of peace cannot be achieved by empty words. It must be obtained through courageous and difficult efforts. Today, as the representatives gather here for this meeting, we should not disappoint the millions of people who are less fortunate than us. The countries that are across the sea from us are constantly cycling through old hatreds and new grievances. When there are unjust or unequal events, they are willing to resort to force rather than peaceful solutions, and believe that the only way to open up new overseas markets is to recover their land. We know that all parties are currently striving to expand armaments, and that millions of men and women must be employed to manufacture weapons. However, this phenomenon is false, and it cannot create a permanent structure. There is no so-called consumption." Mr. Roosevelt solemnly declared that the hope of the whole world still lies in democracy. If we continue to successfully promote it throughout the Americas, it will inevitably become more popular and will surpass all methods that we see as violating human freedom and progress. Mr. Roosevelt ended his speech and appealed in a religious tone, "Let us use our religious faith and spirit to make the peace of the Western Hemisphere increasingly consolidated, and may God help us so that our compatriots in other continents may also share the happiness of peace."

After Mr. Roosevelt finished his speech, he gave a speech at the request of the youth of Argentina, saying that when American youth welcome famous people, they often throw paper scraps, and when there is no paper to throw, they tear up telephone books and use the paper. The situation in Argentina seems to be slightly different, as they all use flowers instead of paper. The warm welcome from the people upon arriving in Argentina this time was the most honorable thing in his life. (Reuters, 1st)

Buenos Aires, Argentina - When Mr. Roosevelt's speech lacked time, Justo's son Libro, the son of Argentine President Justo, shouted "Down with imperialism" in the field and was arrested by the police and expelled from the field. Libro is a communist and was recently deported from Brazil. He disrupted the entire field today. Roosevelt ignored it and continued his speech. (National News Agency, 1st)

Mr. Vayo solemnly declared the "special situation" of the Balearic Islands, and said that the area had been occupied by foreign troops. (Reuters, 2nd)

In particular, Italy, whose people have migrated to the American continent in large numbers, are very interested. (Havas News Agency, 1st)

Spanish Rebels; Use Poison Gas to Fight; Intense Artillery Fire Followed by Melee; Attack on Madrid Unsuccessful 69

Madrid - Our correspondent reports that the Nationalist army launched a large-scale attack on the city yesterday, which was the most fierce since the siege of the capital on the 25th of last month. The artillery used was mostly 155 mm caliber artillery, which fired a total of 1,500 shells in two hours. These shells are said to be poison gas shells, and many militiamen belonging to the government army were poisoned. They were immediately transported back to the rear for treatment. The authorities have not yet determined what kind of gas it is. Although the Nationalist army's offensive was fierce, the militiamen resisted without retreating, and finally repelled the Nationalist army and took advantage of the victory to occupy several important locations. Government officials were therefore quite satisfied. For example, (1) the hospital in the university district in the western suburbs, where the Nationalist army's brigade was stationed, has been destroyed by government artillery fire, but the remnants of the Nationalist army's foreign legion are still resisting and have not retreated. (2) The government army's counter-offensive in the towns of Pozuelo and Humera in the northwest suburbs has also made progress. (3) In the area of ​​Casate Gomba Park, the militiamen have occupied the town of Casate Gamada, and the Nationalist army is retreating towards the Garapites Mountains. In addition, the government army has sent 40 fighter planes to bomb the Nationalist army's lines and shot down several Nationalist army bombers. (Havas News Agency, 2nd)

Madrid - After the government army's counter-offensive won and repelled the rebels, the rebels suddenly bombarded fiercely with gas bombs. The government army was forced to retreat to the Pozuelo area. The rebels are now attacking the capital from the west. The two sides fought hand-to-hand overnight. The rebels claimed to have occupied the village of Boadilla. It is heard that 200 government troops were killed in this one place. Today, the government army attacked the old royal garden, Casa del Campo, with the aim of cutting off the connection between the rebel positions in Humera, Pozuelo, and the University City in the northwest. The rebels claimed to have repelled the attacking government army. The government army lost many people and three Russian-made tanks. The government army claimed that it had obtained a strong air force aid team last week. The number was not specified. It is widely believed that 90 military aircraft have arrived. (Reuters, 2nd)

On the Spanish Civil War, Britain Strictly Adheres to Neutrality: The Arms Embargo Bill Passes the House of Commons; German and Russian Intervention Actions Increase the Severity of the European Situation 71

(London) After lengthy debate in the House of Commons today, and after Sir Archibald Sinclair, leader of the Liberal Party, strenuously defended Soviet Russia, the government's motion to prohibit British ships from carrying arms or ammunition to Spain passed its second reading by a vote of 239 to 132. Before the vote, Conservative MP Mr. James, who had recently inspected Spain, gave a speech stating that both sides were receiving substantial assistance from foreign countries, and the war was no longer a Spanish civil war but had transformed into an international war fought on Spanish soil. When proposing the second reading, Board of Trade President Mr. Runciman stated that since Britain joined the non-intervention agreement, the transport of arms and ammunition to Spain had been completely prohibited. However, several British ships were still transporting munitions to Spain. The rebel side recently declared that they intended to use force to stop the maritime supply of arms to Spain. Spanish warships intercepting such British ships would constitute an act of force, searching them would be an insult, and confiscating them would be an act of violence. If they were granted belligerent rights, then we should allow them to stop and search British ships. Since they have not been granted these rights, we should still use the navy to protect British ships transporting munitions in violation of our stated policy. Once this bill becomes law, Spanish warships will no longer be able to interfere with British ships on the high seas under the pretext of intervention and will be resisted. Norway has followed Britain's example, and France is currently considering this action. Many members of parliament opposed this and raised many questions. Mr. Runciman replied that this measure does not apply to ships registered in the Dominions. He believed the navy would no longer protect ships violating the laws applicable to British merchant ships. Among the Dominions, only the Irish Free State has joined the non-intervention agreement. Whether there is any difference in not including Dominion ships is a matter of speculation. To the government's knowledge, no Dominion ships are sailing near Spain. Mr. Runciman finally urged the parliament to pass this bill in one day. Labour MP Mr. Peake moved to oppose the bill because Britain was the only country doing this, and the bill did not consider the point that British ships could transport munitions to Spain via Portugal. In British history, this bill is unprecedented. The government should consult with the governments of the various Dominions before making a decision. He heard the President of the Board of Trade say that ships that act on their own and violate British law by engaging in prohibited activities will not be protected by the British fleet. Labour is extremely concerned about the impact of this procedure. Labour also believes that this type of legislation should be determined after consultation with other governments that have joined the non-intervention agreement.

Foreign Secretary Mr. Eden then joined the debate, saying that the Admiralty had not issued an order not to protect Dominion ships, nor would it want to do so in the future. Therefore, Dominion ships would be protected by the British Navy. Currently, no Dominion shipping routes approach Spain. However, if we suspect that any Dominion ships are transporting munitions to Spain, we should notify the relevant government. We have no reason to believe that any Dominion will not cooperate with our non-intervention policy. For practical reasons, the Spanish war may at some stage grant belligerent rights to both sides. If the other signatories to the non-intervention agreement strictly adhere to the provisions of the agreement, the current situation would not have occurred, as no British ships would be sailing from foreign ports to transport munitions to Spain. We are now trying to stop British ships from transporting munitions from foreign ports, while ships from certain countries are still transporting munitions made in their own countries. We have obtained evidence that certain countries have violated the agreement. It is said that not including the point of transporting munitions to Portuguese ports within the scope of the prohibition is beneficial to the rebels. According to the International Non-Intervention Adjustment Committee, two cases accusing Portugal were not processed due to insufficient evidence. The British government has telegraphed the British representative in Lisbon to investigate everything, and his reply still states that no evidence has been obtained that the Portuguese government has violated the agreement. Those countries that have not adhered to the non-intervention agreement are not making a sincere contribution to European peace. The British representative to the committee will clarify our concerns on this issue tomorrow and will propose expanding the scope of the agreement to prohibit foreign volunteers from going to fight in Spain. Britain's adherence to neutrality allows its humanitarian work to proceed smoothly. The British Navy and consulates have rescued thousands of lives in the war zone, mostly because both sides believe that Britain is the most faithful and neutral of all European countries. Liberal Party leader Mr. Sinclair rose to defend Soviet Russia, saying that the amount of munitions that Soviet Russia transported to Spain before October 15 was limited. It was only when they saw that Italy and Germany were continuously supplying the rebels with munitions and soldiers that they began to supply the Spanish government in large quantities. Therefore, he was indignant at the fact that the Foreign Secretary's speech criticized Soviet Russia more severely than it criticized Portugal or Italy, considering it unfair. (Reuters dispatch, one day)

(Rome) Regarding Spain's application for the League of Nations Executive Council to convene a temporary meeting, semi-official sources recently stated that the general situation is quite serious, but Italy has not given up hope for the fate of Europe as a whole. Previously, when Italy used force against Abyssinia, Prime Minister Mussolini did his best to prevent the Italo-Abyssinian War from spreading to Europe. Later, this promise was kept. Today, Italy's position is better than before, and it should continue to work to prevent the Spanish Civil War from turning into an international war, thereby avoiding a catastrophe for Europe. (Havas dispatch, one day)

(Berlin) Regarding the news circulating in London that 2,000 German soldiers had landed in Cadiz to assist the Nationalists, political circles here remained silent on the matter. However, an official from the propaganda department denied the claim today that German soldiers had landed in Spain, saying that it might have been a misreporting of German immigrants. (Reuters dispatch, two days)

A Record of Inspecting Suiyuan (Continued): Our Troops in Eastern and Northern Suiyuan Have Very Solid Defense Lines; Captured a Great Deal of Military Supplies When Taking Bai Ling Miao 74

The Current Situation of Bai Ling Miao

After our army completely recaptured Bai Ling Miao at 9 AM on the 24th, Sui Chairman Mr. Fu Zuoyi held a banquet on the evening of the 25th for the comfort groups from Ping, Hu, Shanxi, and the Northeast. During the banquet, when Bai Ling Miao was mentioned, some representatives of the comfort groups immediately suggested that they would like to go and inspect and comfort the soldiers. Mr. Fu said that the traffic to the temple was extremely difficult, with many potholes, and he was concerned that everyone would not be able to bear the severe cold. However, if they insisted on going, the provincial government could provide transportation. Upon hearing this, the representatives decided to go at all costs and decided to depart early (26th) morning. The provincial government appointed Mr. Chen Zhiqu, an officer from the Department of Social Affairs, to accompany and take care of them. At 7 AM on the 26th, Mr. Chen led a large car provided by the provincial government to the Suiyuan Hotel. The car was an open-top type, covered with a canvas canopy and equipped with felt blankets inside. It departed from the hotel at about 9 AM, heading directly northwest. After traveling about 20 miles, passing Wugongba, it entered the Daqing Mountains. The climate suddenly turned cold, and the car had great difficulty traveling due to the high and low mountains. Although the representatives were thinly clothed, they still rallied their spirits to move forward. Because the car had a canopy to shield their view, they saw very little along the way. Although the distance from Suiyuan to the temple is said to be 360 miles, the distances in the outer areas have not been officially measured, so it is actually more than 400 miles. The group arrived in Wuchuan at 3 PM, where County Magistrate Chang Weixing, Garrison Brigade Commander Sun Lanfeng, and Chief of Staff Yuan Qingzeng came out to greet them. They were invited to lunch at the county government. After the meal, they continued north. At about 7 PM, they arrived at Erfenzijiao, where Garrison Division Commander Sun Changsheng and Deputy Division Commander Sun Weiming welcomed them. Mr. Sun said that it was late, and the weather was very cold, so it might be inconvenient to travel. He wanted to invite the representatives to get out of the car and rest, but the representatives were afraid that they would not be able to return the next day, so they decided to proceed slowly. Commander Sun, for the sake of safety along the way, used wireless telegraph to notify the garrison, using red and green lights as signals, and approved them to pass at any time. The car traveled for a short time, and it was already dark. The checkpoints along the way were very strict. From Erfenzijiao to the temple was only a 60-mile journey, but they took a wrong turn and detoured for more than 100 miles. It was not until 10:30 PM that they arrived at the temple. Regiment Commander Liu Jingxin, who was stationed at the temple, invited the representatives to stay at the former site of the Special Affairs Office. Everything in the room was as clean as before. Mr. Liu then ordered the preparation of white flour, large flatbreads, and pickles for everyone to eat together. After the meal, Mr. Liu called over several captured and surrendered bandits, and the representatives questioned them about their experiences as bandits and before and after the battle. It was midnight before they rested. Because of the cold and the lack of luggage, many people huddled or walked around the room, waiting for dawn. At about 5 AM on the 27th, the whole group went to the temple to visit. Around the temple were more than a thousand small white houses where the lamas lived. It was surrounded by mountains on all sides, and the temple was built in the western part of the square. At about 7 AM, Regiment Commander Liu prepared a dozen horses for the representatives to ride to the east and west mountain tops to visit the battlefield. The bandit corpses and dead horses abandoned in the battlefield were everywhere, and many had not yet been buried. The local Mongolian dogs were extremely fierce, so the bodies of people and horses were mostly torn and chewed, and were in a state of disrepair. The fortifications abandoned by the bandits on each mountain top were all made of stone. The group returned to the temple at 9 AM. Because the bandit planes came to bomb the temple every day at 10 AM, and there were still four planes that came to drop bombs the day before the group arrived at the temple, everyone took the original army car back at 9 AM. The wind and sand were stronger than when they came, and the yellow sand hit their faces, causing excruciating pain. It was not until about 8 PM that night that they returned to Guihua. Bai Ling Miao is located in the northwest of Sui Province and is an important military area. If it fell into the hands of the bandits, Suiyuan would be under threat at all times. The bandits also regarded the temple as a base for going west to Baotou and south to harass Suiyuan. The bandits repeatedly attacked Suiyuan's eastern Xinghe and Taolin without success, and concentrated all their efforts on the temple, regarding it as a key area for advancement. Because the authorities recognized the military importance of the temple, they had long been determined to recover it. After active planning by Chairman Fu Zuoyi, they launched a feigned attack on the afternoon of the 22nd. The bandit spies received the news and prepared all night, but seeing no action, they thought that our side had no ability to attack, so they did not care. On the 23rd, our army advanced in two routes, and another surprise force combined infantry, cavalry, and artillery to launch a simultaneous attack on the mountain tops of the temple. The mountain pass in front of the temple had the momentum of one man guarding the pass and ten thousand men unable to pass. Our army bravely pounced on the mountain tops, losing more than a dozen times. Until 5 AM (23rd), our army used two armored vehicles to guide ten heavy military vehicles to charge from the front. Each vehicle had 10 to 20 soldiers, each holding machine guns and shooting forward. At this time, our surprise force's encircling troops also occupied an advantageous position at 7 AM and charged in together. At this point, the bandits could not hold out and fled northeast. After our army charged into the temple, two drivers of the armored vehicles were dead and one was injured. Ten people in the heavy vehicles, six dead and two injured. Six or eight soldiers on each vehicle were also injured or killed. At that time, some of the bandits had not yet escaped and were captured. Our army participating in this campaign included Zhao Chengzhou's cavalry, Sun Changsheng's division, and Sun Lanfeng's less-than-a-brigade number of Fu Zuoyi's troops. After our army arrived at the temple, another infantry unit was sent to pursue. Before leaving, the bandits set fire to some gasoline and military supplies.

Consolidating the Temple Defense

In total, the military supplies accumulated by the bandits in the temple over the years were captured by our side, including three flat rooms of gasoline, tens of thousands of bags of Fengtian-made 65 bullets, 6-700 guns, and countless wireless telegram intelligence documents. Everything in the bandit barracks and offices remained as it was. Some guns and clothes were still hanging on the walls. It can be seen that they did not anticipate our army's surprise attack. When Mr. Fu issued the attack order, he stayed up all night, listening for information from the front at any time. He also received information that the bandits had 5,000 men coming from the west to provide support, so he paid more attention. It was not until he received a telegram on the morning of the 24th that Bai Ling Miao had been recaptured that he felt relieved. (1st)

A Great Fire at Dashatou, Guangzhou; More Than a Hundred Wooden Houses Reduced to Ashes; Hundreds of Refugees Huddling in the Streets 75

Guangzhou Communication, Since entering autumn in Guangdong Province, there has been a long drought and no rain, coupled with high winds and dry objects. Citizens are not careful with fire, resulting in repeated fires, with losses of tens of thousands of yuan. This is a problem that deserves attention in society. Moreover, the locations of the fires are mostly slums. Once a disaster occurs, refugees are displaced, and the rubble fields have been unable to recover construction for a long time. The tragic situation is much worse than ordinary fires. Unexpectedly, after the two major fires in Dongguan Xinshengsha and Henan Huaxie Mountain, a fire broke out in Dashatou on the 29th of this month, burning 119 stores and hundreds of homeless poor people. Dashatou is located at the eastern end of the Guangzhou East Bund, separated from the Bund by a strip of water, no different from a small island. It was formerly the third district of Panyu County and was only划入Guangzhou's police area last year, under the jurisdiction of the former Jian Branch. The area is formed by the accumulation of sand, hence the name Dashatou. Nearby ships are like ants, surrounded by water on all sides. The scenery is beautiful. In recent years, due to various economic downturns, it feels bleak. Only a few hundred wooden houses remain along the coast, all of which are workers' residences or fishing households, with low walls and eaves arranged in a scale-like pattern. Last year, the authorities once planned to turn the area into an entertainment area and gambling place, but the matter did not succeed due to the political turmoil. Recently, a certain bank has acquired land there and plans to build a residential area to prosper the area. Dashatou is indeed a good urban area of the future.

The fire started at the Hefahao iron nail factory on Shab North Street. The factory had more than 20 workers. The factory's construction was made of wooden fir planks. At about 12 o'clock on the 29th, due to cooking lunch, the stove fire flew up and burned the plank wall. In a moment, it became unbearable. When the neighbors alerted the police and fire trucks gathered, it was difficult to rescue them due to the narrow streets. Later, the Jinghua fire-fighting ship on the water surface arrived to assist in the rescue. It was not until 2 PM that the fire was extinguished. When the flames were soaring, the residents fled in embarrassment. Several people were burned by the fire, and several people were injured in falls. They were sent to the convenience hospital for treatment by the rescue team. After the investigation, the burnt stores are as follows: On Shab North Street, the shops and households that were burned, from door number 1 to number 54, totaled 54. On Qiaobian Street, from number 1 to number 32, a total of 32 stores were destroyed. On Dongchuanlan, from number 1 to number 13, a total of 13 were destroyed. On Shab South Street, from number 1 to number 20, a total of 20 were destroyed. The above four streets, a total of 119 rooms were burned. In addition, nearby shipyards burned down six or seven ships of various sizes. That night, more than 530 refugees huddled in the streets, which was very pitiful. The Shan Hospital immediately sent staff to transport dry food and cotton clothes to distribute relief. (November 30)

Hubei Provincial Government Prepares to Hand Over; Huang Shaohong Will Come to Hubei to Take Office; Wuhan Continues to Experience Disturbing Public Security Cases; Newly Appointed Garrison Commander Guo Chan Scheduled to Take Office 76

Hankou Communication, Since the assassination of the late Chairman Yang Yongtai of the Hubei Provincial Government, Mr. Lu Zhu, a member and secretary-general of the Central Committee, was immediately appointed by telegram to act as chairman. Therefore, all government affairs proceeded as usual and were not interrupted. As for the selection of a successor as chairman, there was much speculation from the outside world. The Central Committee believed that Hubei was in an important position and needed to select someone carefully. After delaying for more than a month, it was decided to transfer Mr. Huang Shaohong, Chairman of Zhejiang, to take office. It is said that it has been approved at an Executive Yuan meeting one day, but the date of Mr. Huang's arrival in Hubei to take office will have to wait until the handover of the Zhejiang Provincial Government is completed before it can be determined. However, it can be arrived at Hubei by mid-month at the latest. Before Mr. Huang's arrival, the provincial government affairs will still be carried out by Acting Chairman Lu Zhu. Mr. Lu has instructed all responsible personnel to prepare for the handover. However, this is a transfer of the chairman, not a reorganization of the provincial government. The committee members and department heads may not undergo many changes. On the eve of Mr. Huang's announcement of his transfer to Hubei, the Wuhan Garrison Commander was also ordered to change. The former commander, Mr. Chen Jicheng, was promoted to the director of the Henan, Hubei, and Shaanxi Border Area, responsible for maintaining stability in the border area. The organization of the common office and the location have not yet been determined. Mr. Chen has telegraphed Chairman Chiang to ask for instructions. The newly appointed commander, Mr. Guo Chan, formerly the chief of staff of the 18th Army, recently arrived in Hubei from Guangdong and is scheduled to take office on the 10th. During the transition period between the old and new commanders, three public security disturbance cases occurred in Wuhan in the past two days: (1) The giant robbery case of the Jukang pawn shop in Houhualou, Hankou. Four bandits, each armed with a handgun, completely robbed the shop at 10 PM on the 30th. By the time the police arrived, the bandits had already fled far away and could not be apprehended. (2) The assassination case in Yifeng Alley, Wuchang. The victims were the aunt and nephew of the Wang family, residents of No. 3. Both were fatally wounded and died. One suspect was arrested at the scene. (3) The kidnapping case of Guo Wenyu, the young owner of Qixin Photo Studio on Jianghan Road, Hankou. Guo was only seven years old. He was kidnapped from the shop on the 29th and a ransom of 5,000 yuan was demanded. One bandit was arrested one day, but Guo had already been killed. Wuhan's public security has been well maintained in recent years, with very few robbery and murder cases. Kidnapping and killing of hostages is even unheard of. During the winter defense period, three major cases occurred in two days, and all of them were in the bustling city, which cannot but attract attention.

Hai Cheng: Bandit Chief Hong Datou Killed; The 157th Division Denies Incorporating Huang Guotai 77

Xiamen Communication, The bandits in Zhangzhou, especially the small groups in Haicheng, Fuxi, and Zhangpu, are the most brutal, rampaging through the townships of the three counties and often at sea in Zhangma. Haicheng is indeed a den of musk. There are groups led by Huang Guotai, Hong Datou, Guo Loukong, Zheng Beizai, Huang Adong, Chen Lianqing, Chen Quan, Huang Gansheng, Qiu Lian, Zheng Ba, Zheng Qingzhi, Gan Meihua, and Longxi, led by Jiang Tiansi, and Zhangpu, led by Zhang Baoxiang and Lan Cang, with each group having dozens or more than ten or twenty people. Huang Guotai, who has a certain background, is the leader. Among the groups, Guotai's direct bandit unit, Hong Datouzhong, Guo Loukong, and Zheng Beizai are larger and the most brutal. Zheng was killed by the former defense army's 75th Division in early October, and the remnants were led by Huang Guotai. After the 157th Division took over the defense of southwestern Fujian, it actively suppressed Guotai and other groups. On November 28, the 942nd Regiment of the 471st Brigade of the division killed the bandit leader Hong Datou in Jiaojiao, Haicheng County. The regiment learned that Hong Datou had led his troops to hide in Jiaojiao, Daqiqian, the intersection of Zhangpu and Haicheng. On the night of the 27th, he rushed from the county seat overnight and surrounded him in three routes. Hong led more than 40 bandits to resist in a panic. After fierce fighting until the morning of the 28th, Hong was shot and killed in battle. The remaining bandits fled. Yang Louchang and He Gugui were captured. Hong's body was taken to the county government for public display. Two Mauser pistols were seized. Hong's body was shown to the public. Yang and He were shot dead on the morning of the 29th. Hong Datou once killed Chen Wenpin, the fourth district chief of Zhangpu, and killed the entire family of more than a dozen people of Su Yuqi, the director of the Dongmentou Joint Security. He usually robbed, kidnapped, and killed, doing everything possible, which was hated by the people of Chengpu. In addition, Hong Datou's bandit life was extremely extravagant, with one wife and two concubines, and he also had a lot of bandit property. It is heard that the authorities plan to confiscate the bandit property for public use. Recently, the local newspapers reported that the 157th Division would incorporate Huang Guotai, Hong Datou, Huang Hedong, and other bandits. Mr. Li Yupei, director of the division's political training office, met with reporters on the 30th and formally denied the proposal. Guotai has a certain background and is extremely brutal. His harm to the people is greater than that of the major bandits in southwestern Fujian. On November 16, Huang Adong and Lan Cang attacked the office building of Wudan Village, Xia Palace Society, in the first district of Zhangpu, because they failed to collect more than 5,000 yuan, killing Chief Yang Zhi and as many as 39 villagers, men, women, and children. It was indeed a great catastrophe. (December 2)

Kunshan Consolidating the Collection of Two Terms of Land Tax 78

The land registration of this county has been completed, and household registers and field books have been compiled. The method has been changed to sequential numbering by household. However, due to the short timeframe, it has been decided to consolidate the collection of the first and second terms of land tax. Collection will begin on the first of this month, with five collection points set up throughout the county, located in towns such as Lujia浜, Qiandun, Yangxiangjing, Jiaozhi, and Bacheng. It is stipulated that landowners must pay at their respective locations to avoid malfeasance. The detailed tax rates have also been determined: First-class top-grade land will be taxed at $1.22 per mu, middle-grade at $1.10, and low-grade at $0.98. Second-class top-grade land will be taxed at $0.86, middle-grade at $0.74, and low-grade at $0.61. Third-class top-grade land will be taxed at $0.49, middle-grade at $0.37, and low-grade at $0.25. It is anticipated that this year's harvest will be abundant, and tax revenue will be better than in previous years.

Military Supply Officer Flees with Funds 79

Li Zuolin, the supply officer of the 9th Battalion of the Security Forces stationed in Kunshan, has held his position for many years. Recently, he suddenly absconded with over 3,000 yuan of public funds and disappeared without a trace. The authorities have detained Li's wife, Cai, for investigation.

Changshu Arrest of Suspected Traitors 80

The Second Branch Bureau of Public Safety arrested four suspected traitors in the Zhizhang town of the Fifth District on the first of the month. According to their statements, they are named Zhang Jintao, Xia Quannan, Lu Binbei, and Zhu Xingsheng. They claimed to have come from Shanghai to Changshu for sightseeing and have no fixed destination. These individuals were dressed in Western-style suits of various colors and spoke evasively. They had been loitering in the town for several days, and their behavior was highly suspicious. They were immediately taken into custody and sent to the county jail that evening.

Wuxi Police Bureau Examines Female Police Officers 81

The Public Safety Bureau of this county, for the sake of protecting women and children, maintaining public morals, and facilitating household registration, formally examined female police officers at 8:30 AM yesterday to select three official appointees and six alternates. The examination, led by the chief of the First Section, Lin Kai, tested four subjects: Party Principles, Chinese Language, General Knowledge, and English. A total of seven candidates took the exam, including Wang Peidi, Chen Liangyu, Zhou Xuan, Han Zhiyun, Li Lixue, Zou Shujing, and Wang Fenyuan. All of them have a good chance of being selected. Director Zhang stated that because the number of female candidates was small, it was insufficient for allocation, so another examination will be held on the fifth of this month.

Soldier Shoots Himself 82

Di Jianpei, a first-class soldier of the Second Company of the Sixth Battalion of the Provincial Security Forces stationed in Wuxi, was 31 years old and from Liyang. He was responsible for guarding the Second Company headquarters at Nanchansi Temple under the Nanmen Pagoda Bridge. Several days ago, Di committed a mistake and was ordered by his superior officer to kneel as punishment for two hours. Di felt extremely ashamed and humiliated, and the thought of suicide arose in his mind. Yesterday morning around 6 AM, Di took a rifle, pretending to go to the nearby toilet, but unexpectedly shot himself. With a loud bang, Di fell to the ground, dead on the spot, lying stiff in a pool of blood. The bullet entered his abdomen and exited his shoulder blade. The battalion adjutant, Hu Dun, notified the deceased's cousin, Di Tingheng, to prepare a coffin for burial. It was truly tragic.

Agricultural Bank Loans Secured by Rice 83

The Farmers Bank of this county, in order to benefit farmers, has specially established agricultural warehouses in Dongting, Qianqiao, Anzhen, Yanqiao, and other places to store rice and wheat. Now that the new rice from various villages has been put on the market, the Farmers Bank has decided to start providing loans secured by rice, starting yesterday. Each dan (unit of weight) will be calculated at 70% of the market price, with a monthly interest rate of 1.5%. It is said that the bank plans to lend 100,000 yuan in Dongting and 50,000 yuan in other locations, so that the rural economy can be adequately supported.

Zhenjiang Surveying Riverbank Collapse 84

The riverbank along the Yao Port area in Nantong has been collapsing for years due to water erosion, and the situation is quite severe. Breakwaters were built years ago, but they are now in a precarious state. Peng, the director of the county's Construction Bureau, has drafted a plan to repair and protect the collapsing riverbank and submitted it to the Construction Department for review. It is reported that Director Shen considers this project important and has specially dispatched supervising engineer Zhou Kebao to work with Jiang Diquan, an engineer from the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, to inspect the river flow direction and measure the flow rate in various ports in Nantong in order to plan for bank protection.

Water Police Tightens Fishery Protection 85

The Third District Division of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Corps considers the Shengsi Islands under the jurisdiction of Chongming County to be the most important fishing area in Jiangsu Province. Every winter during the ribbonfish season, patrol ships are dispatched to maintain order and protect fishermen's businesses. However, since the Bảo vệ Đoàn (Defense Corps) rebellion, the area's vitality has been greatly damaged and its strength has not been restored. During this fishing season, comprehensive consideration is necessary to ensure safety. With the fishing season approaching, the Division is making careful plans for protection and actively implementing them. The Division has invited the County Magistrate of Chongming and the fleet commander of the District Division to discuss protection measures. Detailed arrangements have been made for fleet deployment, departure times, command and dispatch, and coordination and support.

Danyang Patricide Case Adjudicated 86

Mao Xiaohai, a resident of Erling Township, was angered by his father's gambling and stabbed him to death with a knife last month. The district office reported the incident to the county government, which sent officials to investigate and arrested the suspect, Mao Xiaohai, for interrogation and imprisonment. Yesterday, the county government issued its verdict: Mao Xiaohai is sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment and ten years of deprivation of civil rights for intentionally causing the death of a direct lineal ascendant.

Nantong Major Robbery Case Solved 87

Four thousand yuan in cash, being transported by the Tongcheng Company to the Wantonghe Cotton Firm in Jugang, was robbed by four bandits in the Fangquanbu area. Police officers chased and apprehended two bandits, Ji Changfu and Ding Jihe, and recovered 1,300 yuan. The two bandits at large were identified as Squad Leader Sun and Li of the Tax Police District. Peng Longrang, the Deputy Commander of the Fourth District Security Headquarters, along with Wang Zhisan, the Adjutant of the Tax Police District, conducted a thorough investigation and detained Sun and Li. The missing cash was also recovered. The four bandits are currently being transported from Rugao by the Security Forces to the District Security Headquarters for interrogation.

Nanjing Chinese Society for the Study of Reason 88

The Chinese Society for the Study of Reason, in light of the soldiers fighting bandits in the icy and snowy conditions of Suiyuan, has sent a nationwide appeal to all members to donate generously and directly send funds to the front lines for comfort.

Linhuai Chamber of Commerce Recalls Circulation Notes 89

The Chamber of Commerce of this town, in accordance with orders from this spring to repair the Guangyun Bridge and collect land rent, has been recalling the circulation notes issued by the Chamber in 1927. The Chamber has repeatedly notified all sectors to recall the notes in installments according to the approved method. It has been found that the funds for the first phase of the notes have already been paid out, but there are still some registered but uncollected notes. It is proposed to set a deadline to complete the recall and then submit the notes to the county for cancellation. All holders of these circulation notes, regardless of whether they have registered or not, are required to present them for exchange within two weeks from today. If they fail to do so by the deadline, the Chamber will report the completion and the notes will no longer be redeemable.

Huoqiu Developing West Lake Wasteland 90

The Anhui provincial authorities have been determined to develop water conservancy projects and reclaim wasteland in recent years, sparing no effort. Significant results have been achieved in irrigation projects. The development of West Lake in Huoqiu is a prime example of this success. West Lake is located in the near suburbs of Huoqiu County and is a famous scenic spot in northern Anhui. The lake covers an area of 430 square li, totaling 7,000 qing, of which 4,000 qing are already cultivated land (including 2,000 qing of government wasteland). The newly dried land and the land still under water each account for over 1,000 qing. In order to develop the lake and turn all the land into arable land, the Anhui provincial government ordered the Huoqiu County government to build the Renjiagou drainage gate and the Xinhe floodgate, as well as culverts at Longwokou and Guanzhoukou. The government also ordered the dredging of the Lihe River, Wangjieliu River, and Xinhe River, and the raising of the lake's dikes. Construction of the culverts and floodgates will be funded by the county government, while the levees will be raised using civilian labor without compensation. It is reported that after a year, the construction of the West Lake culverts and floodgates and the dredging and raising of the dikes have been completed. The reclamation of the land within the lake is being implemented in stages, and sections 2, 3, and 4 are nearing completion. Construction of sections 1, 5, and 6 will officially begin on December 1, with over 9,000 laborers recruited. Officials from the Huoqiu County government will supervise and assist in the project. When completed next year, 1,500 qing of fertile land can be reclaimed. The government wasteland will be leased for 200 yuan per qing, which will bring in 300,000 yuan in one go. If the government operates its own agricultural farms and hires tenants, each qing will produce 1,000 yuan annually, increasing production capacity by 2 million yuan per year, which will greatly benefit agriculture. The development of East Lake in the eastern suburbs of Huoqiu is also being planned.

Xuzhou Two Department Directors Visit Xuzhou 91

Yu Jingtang, the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, and Zhao Dihua, the Director of the Department of Finance, arrived in Xuzhou on the Shanghai-Ping-Tong train on the evening of the 27th to inspect civil affairs, finance, sanitation, and opium suppression in the Xuzhou and Huai areas. They were accompanied by Yuan Chen, the director of the provincial hospital, Wang Maoqing, an accounting specialist, and Fang Yuanminshou, the director of the anti-opium commission. They stayed at the Huayuan Hotel. Leaders from various sectors visited them that evening. The next morning, Yu and Zhao jointly inspected the local institutions. At noon, they inspected the壮丁(strong recruits) and public security police at the public sports field under Yunlong Mountain. That afternoon, they traveled by car to Xiao County, first detouring to Gushan Baitu Village to inspect the Dazhong Coal Mine and go down into the mine. They then proceeded to Xiaocheng to inspect various institutions and people's factories. They also visited the Daihe First Bridge and praised the spirit of construction in Xiao County. They returned to Xuzhou on the evening train. This morning (30th), they traveled by car to Sui County and then to Suqian, inspecting the Huai area before returning to the province.

Letter 92

To the esteemed editor,

I have just read the news item in your December 1st issue regarding a communication from Fengjing about brothers fighting over their inheritance, and I am deeply shocked. The truth is that I and Rongchu are brothers with a close relationship, and there has never been any discord between us. As for the inheritance, my late father had already divided it fairly while he was still alive and established separate households for us. There has been no conflict whatsoever. Furthermore, I am content with my lot and have no bad habits. My annual income is sufficient to support myself, so how could I be so devoid of conscience as to engage in such heartless acts? The claim that I have squandered my resources and am forcefully seizing my brother's inheritance is clearly a malicious slander. In addition to requesting your newspaper to correct this immediately, I will also take legal action to protect my rights. This matter concerns my personal reputation, so I am writing to you specifically to request a correction.

Sincerely,

Shen Liuchu of Fengjing, December 2nd

Local News

Various Organizations Hold Public Banquet for Hu Shi Last Night; Hu Delivers Public Speech After Dinner; Attendance Is High and No Space Is Left 93

Last night at 6:30 PM, the Shanghai International Problems Research Association, the Banking Association, the Money Trade Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Youth Association, the Local Association, the World Chinese Students' Federation, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the International Settlement, the Pacific International Society, the Joint Association of University Faculty, the Public Welfare Promotion Association, and the Shen Bao newspaper jointly held a public banquet at the Eight Immortals Bridge Youth Association for Hu Shi, the Chinese representative to the Pacific Science Congress. Those in attendance included Lin Kanghou, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Huang Renzhi, Lu Bohong, Weng Zhilong, Ou Yuanhuai, Liu Yuwan, Li Dachao, Zhu Shaoping, Zhang Ganchen, Zhang Shouyong, Liu Zhanen, Dai Baoliu, Cao Yunxiang, and Ma Yinliang, among dozens of others. The atmosphere was convivial, and the guests and hosts enjoyed themselves. After dinner, Hu Shi went to the auditorium to deliver a public speech titled "Thoughts on Returning." The audience was extremely enthusiastic, and latecomers were unable to enter. Liu Zhanen first introduced Hu Shi's speech, saying that the mission to the United States was twofold: one was to attend the Sixth Pacific International Congress, and the other was to represent Peking University, Nankai University, and the Academia Sinica at the Harvard University Tercentenary. The biggest takeaway from the Harvard University Tercentenary was that each representative was given a booklet listing the academic institutions they represented, each with a number corresponding to the institution's founding date. Peking University was listed as number 419, Nankai University as number 454, and the Academia Sinica as number 499. There were only five numbers below that, and he deeply felt that our five-thousand-year-old culture was so backward. In ancient times, we had the establishment of the Taixue (Imperial Academy), and during the Eastern Han Dynasty, there were over 30,000 students at the Taixue. The early establishment and large number of students surpassed those of European schools today. Unfortunately, our ancient schools lacked continuity, and the principals and professors were all government officials and could not be separated from politics, so the academic atmosphere and cultivation of talent could not continue. The success of European universities today is due to the fact that their leaders and talents all come from universities. The European Renaissance, the Reformation, and the research of new sciences were all led by figures who came from universities. The difference between them and us lies in the presence or absence of universities. Only five were listed after us, such as Princeton University, where people like Einstein came from. Students at the California Institute of Technology have even won the Nobel Prize. This is sufficient proof that even if the founding date is late, it is not too late to catch up. As for the Pacific International Congress, it was held in Yosemite, California, which was formerly a Spanish imperial territory. Today, the Spanish Civil War is still ongoing, and the future is bleak. This is sufficient to show that empires that rely solely on military force and lack cultural and industrial foundations cannot last. Facts are the most powerful form of propaganda. Three years ago, at the Pacific Conference, countries were indifferent to the situation in the Far East. Today, countries have economic conflicts with Japan and feel threatened. The peace of the Pacific is no longer guaranteed. Now, countries are either adopting reciprocal agreements, boycotting Japanese imports, or increasing import taxes to cope. At the same time, in military and political terms, the Pacific Rim countries are expanding their military forces. This proves that the facts created by Japan outweigh countless propaganda efforts. American public opinion has undergone a major change. From 1914 to 1931, Japan dominated the Pacific. During the European war, that was of course the case. Although the Washington Conference resulted in restrictions on Japan, its hegemony was still recognized by all countries. However, after the September 18th Incident, Japan abused its hegemony and made it a harmful thing, thereby triggering: (1) the Soviet Union's attention to the East, (2) the increase in military forces in Pacific countries outside of Asia, and (3) China's awakening and the completion of unification. What the future will bring is difficult to predict, but seeking help from others is ultimately an illusion. Constantly creating facts is the real interest and can give people a deeper feeling. Tonight at 8 PM, the Shanghai International Problems Research Association, the Returned Students Association, the Pan-Pacific Society, the Joint Association of University Faculty, and the Pacific International Society will host a banquet for Hu Shi at the International Hotel. At that time, Hu Shi will deliver a speech in English on "The Evolving Pacific."

Women's Circles Establish Suiyuan Anti-Bandit Comfort Association Yesterday; Elect 33 Directors, Each Family Should Donate at Least One Vest as Cold Weather Supplies 94

Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, the Shanghai Suiyuan Anti-Bandit Soldiers Comfort and Relief Committee and the Relief Undertaking Advancement Association hosted a reception for women from all circles at the Local Association. Huang Renzhi reported on the relief situation and progress in Suiyuan, Qian Xinzhi reported on the cold weather in Suiyuan, and Li Dachao spoke about expanding the collection of winter clothing.

Resolutions Passed

The following proposals were discussed: (1) The proposal to raise cold-weather supplies was resolved as follows: (A) Schools will collect at least one pair of gloves per student and one vest per household. (B) Organizations and individuals will be contacted separately for donations. (C) Households will focus on donating vests. (2) The proposal on the types of cold-weather supplies to be raised was resolved as follows: (A) 50,000 vests, (B) 100,000 pairs of gloves, (C) 100,000 pairs of earmuffs, (D) cash. (3) The proposal on the deadline for collection was resolved to be December 15th. (4) The proposal on collection points was resolved to be at the Young Women's Christian Association. (5) The proposal to organize the Shanghai Women's Circle Suiyuan Bandit Extermination Comfort Association was passed to merge and expand with the former Women's Circle organization. (6) The temporary meeting place was set at the Local Association. (7) Thirty-three temporary staff members were selected and divided into three groups: fundraising, publicity, and design. (8) Expenses will be raised by the committee members. (9) On-the-spot donations of cold-weather supplies will be solicited. (10) Prominent figures in society will be invited as consultants. (11) The first meeting of the board of directors will be held at the Local Association at 4:30 PM on Friday.

Collection Method

The following collection methods were adopted yesterday: (1) Collect 100,000 pairs of gloves (preferably thick flannel or wool). (2) Collect 50,000 vests (gray cloth for the outer layer, silk cotton for the lining, at least half a jin). The materials used should be domestic products. The price of gloves should be around 20 to 30 cents, and the price of vests should be around $1.50. (3) Schools should focus on collecting gloves. (4) Households should focus on collecting vests. (5) Organizations and individuals should also send people to contact and confirm the types and quantities of donations. (6) It is hoped that students from elementary to high school will donate several pairs of gloves. (7) Donors who can make these gloves and vests themselves are welcome. If they hire workers to make them, they should ask the factory to estimate the cost and pay accordingly. (8) Due to the urgent military situation, it is planned to collect all supplies by December 15th. (9) The collection points are tentatively set at the Local Association, the Vocational Education Society, the Chinese Girls' Middle School, and the Young Women's Christian Association. (10) Receipts should use a uniform format. (11) In order to promote the continued advancement of work, there should be a corresponding organization.

New Buildings for Shanghai Medical Affairs Undertakings Completed in Succession; Ninth Meeting Held Yesterday 97

The Shanghai Medical Affairs Board of Directors held its ninth meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday in the new campus meeting room of the National Shanghai Medical College, located at Shenjia浜 South, Fenglinqiao. Chairman Kong Yongzhi, Minister, and Directors Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Wang Zhengting, Zhao Jinqing, Ma Yinliang, Wen Lanting, Guo Shun, Wu Tiecheng, Zhang Jiguang, Lu Chengzhang, Li Tingan, Yan Fuqing, Xu Xinliu (represented by Yan Fuqing), etc., attended. First, they visited the new buildings of the Medical College and Zhongshan Hospital, and then convened the meeting, chaired by Chairman Kong. First, General Director Yan reported that the construction of the Medical College has been completed, and students in the basic departments have been moved in for classes. In addition, a student dormitory has also been completed. The Songde Hall and Liangcai Hall buildings will both be completed by the end of this month, along with the Zhongshan Hospital building. The original site of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai office, which was purchased previously, has been rebuilt into a graduate nurses' dormitory, and vocational housing is being built on the vacant land. This is a summary of the construction. Next, the financial report was made. The Board of Directors has hired accountant Chao Jimei as an auditor to review the financial income and expenditure, and the construction accounts of Zhongshan Hospital, and prepare a report. After the directors reviewed it, it was approved. In addition, accountant Chao also designed an accounting system for Zhongshan Hospital, which was resolved to be submitted to the Standing Committee. After the report, the following resolutions were passed: (1) The Shenjia浜 Road in front of Zhongshan Hospital, and the Fenglin Road on the side, should be quickly paved with asphalt roads by the Municipal Government to facilitate traffic. In addition, the main gate of the Medical College is planned to be built across Shenjia浜 Road to enhance its grandeur, and will be dismantled and moved back when the road is opened in the future. When the above two motions were passed, Mayor Wu, attending as a director, approved them on the spot. (2) The purpose of Zhongshan Hospital's construction is to serve society, so although the number of beds is large, they are all for the common people. The first-class wards are insufficient, and it is proposed to build another first-class ward building, which will cost 60,000 yuan. How should the funds be raised? It was resolved to build another first-class ward building, named 中正樓(Zhongzheng Building) to commemorate Chairman Chiang, and the expenses will be borne separately by the directors. Detailed methods will be proposed by Directors Kong Yongzhi, Sun Ke, Wu Tiecheng, Qian Xinzhi, Liu Hongsheng, Lin Kanghou, Ye Zichong, and Yan Fuqing. After the discussion, the meeting adjourned. It was late into the evening.

After Brisk Yarn Sales, Yarn Inventory Is Exhausted; Total Is Less Than 10,000 Bales; Truly an Unprecedented Record in Ten Years; Yarn Prices Rise to a New High After 128 98

After yarn sales picked up in various regions, yarn inventory has greatly decreased, reaching a low not seen in ten years. Prices have risen to a new high of 256 yuan. However, due to the lack of national cotton harvests and low Indian cotton prices, a new phenomenon of cheap cotton and expensive yarn has emerged. Details are recorded as follows:

Active Yarn Sales; Inventory Exhausted

Since August,现紗(spot yarn) sales have been consistently good, continuously rising. Even the Tianjin幫(group), which had been inactive for a long time, has been buying in large quantities, causing Shanghai's yarn inventory to decrease greatly. As of the end of September, it was 34,840 bales. By the end of October, it had dropped to 14,240 bales, of which 1,403 bales were from Japanese factories, and 12,837 bales were from Chinese and British factories, a low not seen in nearly ten years. At the same time, the yarn inventory in the warehouses of the Chinese Yarn and Cloth Exchange had decreased to 5,485 bales by the end of October.

Yarn Prices Have Risen to New Highs

In November,现紗(spot yarn) sales continued to be very good. Various yarn factories had already sold a lot of futures in the past two months, so the yarn that they could supply to the market greatly decreased. At the same time, a labor strike occurred in Japanese yarn factories, reducing production by 30% overall. This further reduced the supply to the market, creating a phenomenon where no yarn could be purchased. Last Saturday, sales in Sichuan were very good, causing yarn prices to rise sharply in recent days. In December, each bale had risen to a new high of 256 yuan, unseen since 128.

Strong Cloth Sales Help Yarn Price Increase

As for Shanghai's yarn inventory as of the end of November, it is estimated to have dropped to below 10,000 bales, while the yarn inventory in the warehouses of the Chinese Yarn and Cloth Exchange is only 1,605 bales. The reason for the yarn price increase is entirely due to insufficient production to meet demand, and not due to speculation. As for the cotton weaving factories that use yarn as raw material, their sales are very good due to the good harvests in rural areas across the country and the increased purchasing power of the people. They are already buying spring goods for next year, which is further fueling the yarn price increase.

Creating a New Phenomenon of Cheap Cotton and Expensive Yarn

In the past, cotton did not rise much along with yarn. In recent days, it has risen slightly, mainly because the yarn increase is too great. However, the cotton price increase is still not as high as yarn. The reasons are: (1) Because of the large domestic harvest, it is estimated that there will be a supply of 1.4 million擔(dan), which is calculated to be surplus. (2) Because Indian cotton prices are low, the current Chinese cotton prices are close to Indian cotton prices. If Chinese cotton prices rise further, it will cause Indian cotton imports, so the general public is still bearish on cotton prices. This phenomenon is actually beneficial to the yarn industry. In summary, it is still a reversal of the past five or six years of cheap yarn and expensive cotton.

Rice Industry Representatives Went to Jiading Yesterday to Investigate; Jijiang Temple Detained Rice Boats; Visited County Magistrate Guo to Inquire About the Truth 102

Dagong News Agency reported that the Jijiang Temple Police Station of the Jiading County Public Security Bureau has detained more than 120 rice boats passing through the Wusong Port from Wuxi, Changshu, Wujiang, Kunshan, and other places from 3:00 PM the day before yesterday to 5:00 PM yesterday, and eight or nine wheat boats. The boats are connected end to end in the six or seven里(li) river ports from Huangdu in the east to Beixin泾 in the south. Because the waterway is very shallow, other boats coming and going are blocked. After the news spread to the Beishi rice market in the city, Fu Qianeng, a member of the Shanghai Soybean and Rice Industry Association, Jiang Shizhi, chairman of the Beishi Grain Merchants Association, and Lu Muqin and Shi Zufug, directors of the Changshu Guild Hall, went to the Jijiang Temple area yesterday morning to investigate, and then went to Jiading to meet with County Magistrate Guo and Jin Boqin, chairman of the county chamber of commerce, to inquire about the truth of the detention of transit rice boats. They also requested the immediate release based on the Executive Yuan's resolution on the free circulation of domestic food, in order to maintain the food supply for Shanghai residents. County Magistrate Guo stated that he would immediately telegraph the provincial government for instructions and then release the boats.

Severe Drought in Henan Province; Provincial Committee Came to Shanghai to Request Relief; Banquet Tonight to Report on the Disaster Situation to All Sectors 103

Henan Province is suffering from an extraordinarily severe drought this year. The provincial government sent Chang Zhizhen, a member of the provincial committee and chairman of the provincial relief association, south to request relief. He recently went to Beijing, and then came to Shanghai yesterday afternoon. Zhang Fang, a member of the provincial committee, also came south from the province to assist in the negotiations. A banquet is scheduled to be held to report on the disaster situation to all sectors in the city. Details are recorded as follows:

Banquet Tonight for Leaders from All Sectors

Chang Zhizhen, the representative of Henan Province who came south to request relief, came to Shanghai a few days ago and hosted a banquet for the news media to report on the disaster situation in the province. After briefly contacting leaders of various charitable organizations in the city, he went to Beijing the next day to claim the 300,000 yuan in public bonds promised by the Ministry of Finance, and negotiated with the banking sector in Beijing on the matter of mortgaging cash. He came to Shanghai yesterday afternoon after finishing the matters. At the same time, Zhang Fang, a member of the Henan Provincial Government, also came to Shanghai from the province via Pinghan, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi to assist in the proceedings. After consulting with the Henan Association in Shanghai, it was decided to hold a banquet at the Central Western Restaurant on the 4th to report on the disaster situation to all party, government, and military leaders in the city, as well as leaders of various charitable organizations, and request assistance in disaster relief. After arriving in Shanghai, Zhang went to pay respects to former Executive Duan, and will return to the province with Chang after participating in the public memorial.

Chang Zhizhen Talks About the Recent Situation in Henan

The reporter interviewed Chang yesterday. According to him, Henan Province has made progress in politics and construction since 1920, such as the construction of highways, which have connected the province and neighboring provinces. However, due to financial difficulties, only Xinyang to Huangchuan, Huangchuan to Sanhejian, and Luotong highways have been paved. The rest have a solid roadbed, and the Construction Bureau operates public buses for convenient transportation. As for waterways, they have not been paying attention to them, so there are frequent floods and droughts. The provincial government is also actively working on construction. The province's main products are cotton and tobacco. The farmers have a simple life and can still make ends meet. However, the southwestern border of the province is barren and the people are poor. The province's tax revenue is less than 20 million yuan, and income and expenditure can be balanced, but in case of disasters, assistance from the central government and other regions is required. He is very grateful for the concern shown by all parties during this visit to Shanghai.

Fishery Syndicate Established Early; Participating Banks Paid Up Capital; Bank of China Established a Special Account for Temporary Collection; Meeting Convened on the 6th to Discuss Lending Methods 104

The Fishery Syndicate jointly established by the Ministry of Industry and the Bank of China has already begun investigation work after the establishment of the preparatory office. In order to expedite the loan disbursement, it is planned to officially establish it on New Year's Day next year. A third preparatory meeting is specifically scheduled to be held on the 6th to discuss and decide on the capital of 1 million, and each bank will begin to pay up. Details are recorded as follows:

Expedited Loans and Scheduled Establishment

The Fishery Syndicate Preparatory Office, since the second preparatory meeting, decided to limit the preparation period to three months, and stipulated the preparatory work: (1) Collect 1 million yuan of fishery syndicate funds; (2) Formulate the syndicate's business policy; (3) Draft the syndicate's various rules; (4) Draft the general rules for the organization of various fishery production and sales cooperatives; (5) Investigate the fishery situation and the status of existing fishery cooperatives. The preparatory office has now begun to proceed. It is learned that the Ministry of Industry, in view of the lack of capital for the seasonal fishermen, intends to increase the output of the spring fishing season next year, and therefore plans to shorten the syndicate's preparation work and officially establish it and start lending on January 1 next year.

Preparatory Meeting Convened to Decide

Qian Xinzhi, director of the preparatory office, has already hired Qu Junwei, director of the Shanghai Fishery Guidance Office, and Hua Wenyu, director of the lending department of the Xinhua Bank, as design committee members for various design matters, and hired Cao Erwei and other four people as investigators to be responsible for the investigation work. Now, in order to expedite the preparation work and decide on the early establishment date, it is planned to convene a third preparatory meeting on the 6th to discuss the fishery lending methods and various rules. Wu Dingchang, Minister of Industry, has decided to send Yu Zhenyong, Director of the Fisheries and Animal Husbandry Department, to Shanghai to attend and guide the meeting.

Capital of One Million Deposited in Bank of China

The syndicate's capital is 1 million yuan, with 200,000 yuan of fixed capital, which will be paid by the Ministry of Industry. The circulating capital is 800,000 yuan, divided into 40 shares, with each share being 20,000 yuan. The Bank of China has 120,000 yuan, the Bank of Communications has 100,000 yuan, and the Shanghai Bank, the Jin Cheng Bank, the Continental Bank, the Salt Industry Bank, the Zhongnan Bank, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, the Zhonghui Bank, the Xinhua Bank, and the Four Banks Savings Association each have 60,000 yuan, and the Siming Bank has 40,000 yuan, totaling 800,000 yuan. Before the syndicate is officially established, the Bank of China will open a special account to manage the funds. Each bank has prepared to pay up, and once the official establishment date is determined, the full amount can be paid.

Loans to Begin in the Spring Fishing Season

According to reporters from the Xin Xin News Agency who inquired with banks participating in the syndicate, the official start of lending by the Fishery Syndicate will be before the spring fishing season next year. At that time, the syndicate will be officially established, and various lending methods and investigation work will be ready. As for the lending for the winter fishing season this year, the Zhonghui Bank, the Xinhua Bank, and the Four Banks Savings Association have advanced 120,000 yuan to lend to Shanghai fish market wholesalers and the Yin County Fishery Cooperative, and the applications for loans have been very enthusiastic. Most of them have already been disbursed, and only a few are still under review, but they will also be disbursed soon. The future situation of the loans will be considered, and it may be deducted from the total amount of 1 million yuan for balance.
