Joint Announcement by Two Bureaus 108

Abolition of the Rickshaw Donation System; Public Concession Bureau Continues to Handle Owner Registration

Joint announcement by the Finance Bureau and the Public Concession Bureau: It has been received Municipal Government Order No. 21213, which states: "The rickshaw donation in this city should be paid directly by the rickshaw owner. All donation guarantee and proxy donation systems will expire at the end of this year and should be cancelled immediately. In addition to instructing the Public Concession Bureau and the Finance Bureau separately, you are hereby ordered to jointly issue a public announcement in advance (December 1st) to inform all parties, and to report the handling situation for inspection and verification. This order," etc. Upon receiving this, we should comply with it. All donation guarantee and proxy donation systems for rickshaws in this city should be abolished at the same time at the end of the year 25. From January 1, 26, the owner of each rickshaw must carry a genuine owner certificate and go to our Public Concession Bureau to collect a donation payment license from January 1st to 15th every year, and pay the rickshaw donation to our Finance Bureau every month based on the license. Please do not make mistakes, which may damage your rights. In addition to submitting a report, we hereby issue a joint public announcement so that you may all comply with it. Public Concession Bureau announcement. It has been found that our bureau has been ordered to handle the registration of rickshaw owners and issue certificates. We have previously set a deadline for public announcement in the newspaper, and ordered the industry association to inform all rickshaw owners. The deadline has long passed, and although many have complied with the deadline to register, there are still more than 1,000 vehicles that are waiting and seeing, which is very negligent. Now, in order to accommodate these rickshaw owners, the deadline is extended to December 15th of this year as the final registration deadline. If those who fail to register by the deadline will have their license plates revoked. There will be no further leniency. In addition to submitting a report to the Municipal Government for record, we hereby issue another public announcement. Please do not make a mistake. It is imperative.

Ningbo and Guangdong Native Place Associations Convened Mediation Yesterday Regarding the Dispute Between the Guang Gang Lianyi Hall and the Civilian Boat Porters 110

The Shanghai Civilian Boat Porters Professional Union and the Guang Gang Lianyi Hall have been in dispute over employment issues for two months. The Municipal Social Bureau has handled the matter repeatedly, but it has not been resolved, resulting in the unemployment of more than 100 workers. The Ningbo and Guangdong native place associations in Shanghai, witnessing the stalemate, deeply felt that failing to resolve the issue would affect social security and the livelihoods of workers. Therefore, they initiated a meeting scheduled for the 2nd of this month at the Ningbo Native Place Association, convening responsible representatives from both sides. Representatives from the Trade Union included Wang Wenhao, Han Aqin, Zhu Wenfu, and Qin Ziquan. Representatives from Lianyi Hall included Chen Zuo Hou, Zhao Zelin, Li Shiying, and Gan Yingnan. Mediators included Yu Qiaqing, Zhu Meixian, Mao Heyuan, Zhang Jiguang, Wu Yaqin, and Dong Xinqin from the Ningbo Native Place Association, and Li Dachao, Guo Zhongliang, Chen Fengxian, and Chen Qifen from the Guangdong Native Place Association. Yu Qiaqing, Chairman of the Ningbo Native Place Association, presided over the meeting. After brief reports from both sides, the two native place associations separately inquired about the wishes of both parties. Realizing that the case was complex and could not be resolved through words, the presiding officer proposed that the labor side entrust the entire responsibility to the Ningbo Native Place Association, and the capital side entrust the entire responsibility to the Guangdong Native Place Association, and then the representatives of the two native place associations would discuss a solution. After persuasion, both parties accepted the principle and scheduled another meeting for 4:00 PM on the 4th of this month by the two native place associations.

市聯會Yesterday the Municipal Federation Organized the "One Yuan Aid Suiyuan Movement" Promotion Meeting, Resolving to Telegraph Song Zheyuan to Dispatch Troops to Chahar to Suppress Bandits 113

The First Special District Citizens' Federation convened its fourth representative conference yesterday to discuss the "One Yuan Aid Suiyuan Movement." The conference passed a resolution to form a promotion committee, issue a declaration, and telegraph Song Zheyuan to promptly dispatch troops to Chahar to suppress bandits and pacify the border. The details of each matter are recorded below.

Resolutions Passed: The First Special District Citizens' Federation convened its fourth representative conference at 2 PM yesterday. More than 70 representatives from various district branches attended. Zhang Yichen, Cao Zhigong, and Hu Fengxiang were elected as the presidium. After the presidium reported on various association affairs during the intersession period of the third conference, discussions began. The following resolutions were passed by the conference: (1) Passed the draft of the "One Yuan Aid Suiyuan Movement" Promotion Committee Charter. The resolution was amended and passed item by item. (2) Elected members of the Promotion Committee. The resolution elected Ji Jiannan and 58 others as members. (3) (Omitted). (4) Appointed secretaries of the Promotion Committee. The resolution appointed Zhu Yutao, Zheng Dongshan, and Liang Gengshun as secretaries. (5) Set a date for convening the first meeting of the Promotion Committee. The resolution set the meeting for 2 PM on Saturday, December 5th. (6) Raised funds for the operating expenses of the Promotion Committee. The resolution stipulated that, in accordance with the charter, each branch representative should donate to cover the expenses, temporarily collecting one yuan from each representative. (7) Liu Zhongying proposed a plan for promoting the "One Yuan Aid Suiyuan Movement." The resolution referred the plan to the executive committee for discussion. (8) Each district branch should hold regular elections. The resolution directed the association to notify each branch to hold elections on schedule. (9) Public buses frequently cause accidents, and improvements to the equipment should be suggested. The resolution referred this matter to the executive committee for handling. (10) Telegraph Song Zheyuan to dispatch troops to Chahar to suppress bandits and pacify the border. The resolution was passed.

Reporter from the Continental News Interviews Fessenden Regarding the Municipal Council's Cost Reduction Plan; Funds from the Sale of the Electric Department Nearly Exhausted; Tax Office and Education Office Revisions Will Have Impact 115

The Continental News reports: A reporter from the Continental News interviewed Fessenden, Director-General of the Municipal Council, yesterday (1st), asking whether the Municipal Council would be willing to reconsider the proposals for salary reductions for employees put forward by the Special Economy Committee. Mr. Fessenden replied that the Municipal Council is always willing to study any reasonable suggestions put forward by employees regarding this matter. However, the Municipal Council believes that the proposals put forward by the Special Committee are the only feasible way for the Council to cope with the huge annual deficit. The reporter further inquired about criticisms that the proposals of the Commodity Committee were unfair, especially with regard to lower-level employees, and what criticisms he had of this. Mr. Fessenden replied that this was just an opinion. Mr. Fessenden also stated that the proposal put forward by the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, advocating the complete elimination of subsidies for foreign employees' exchange losses, was too harsh. If this were implemented, it would be equivalent to a 16.4% salary reduction for foreign employees, which would be too large. In the past six or seven years, in order to balance the budget, the Municipal Council has had to draw on reserves, which came from the sale of the Electric Department. The funds have been drawn on year after year, and are almost exhausted. The financial difficulties of the Municipal Council in the future can be imagined from this. The general public's comments on the Municipal Council's cost reduction plan are actually due to the current economic downturn in Shanghai, which has led to this situation. While this is true, it does not fully capture the truth. The main reason why the Municipal Council wants to implement large salary cuts and other cost reduction plans is that in the past seven years, the Municipal Council's income has often been insufficient to cover its expenditures. Since 1927, after the patrolman's tax was reduced from 16% to 14%, the Municipal Council has felt that it is impossible to increase the tax rate. However, judging from the current financial situation of the Municipal Council, even if it is increased, it will still not be able to cover the deficit. The only cost reduction measures that the Municipal Council can implement are to reduce employee salaries and other compensation. The public and Municipal Council employees should consider the cost reduction plan, which includes the proposals submitted by the Special Committee, in its entirety, and should not comment on it based on individual opinions. Chinese and foreign employees of the Municipal Council are still vociferously expressing their opposition to the salary reduction plan. Yesterday afternoon, foreign employees of the Tax Office and foreign employees of the Education Office held separate meetings to listen to the explanation of the Special Committee's report. The consensus of the meeting was that the report was very vague. The employees of the Tax Office have already handed this matter over to the Employees' Union of that office for handling. There are many senior personnel in it, so if there are any revisions, the words issued by that group will be very powerful.

False Report of Death to Defraud Life Insurance Payout; Li Bingjing Has Two Scars on His Head; Removing His Hair-Pressing Cap Confirms He is the Person 117

Li Bingchang, also known as Li Benchu, is currently thirty-two years old and opened the Liyuan Money Shop in Chaoyang County, Guangdong. On May 19th of the 21st year of the Republic of China, he took out a life insurance policy with the Hong Kong branch of the American Foreign Insurance Company for HK$50,000. He stated that if Li were to die in the future, the payout should be given to his wife, Li Liang Zhiying (30 years old, from Shantou) to receive. At that time, the company had a doctor verify Li Bingchang's physique, but Li had two characteristic scars on his head, one on his neck and one on his forehead. These were noted on the document. Li then paid the first

premium of four hundred twenty-three yuan and forty-seven cents. On February 4th of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the Hong Kong Foreign Insurance branch suddenly received a letter from Li Bingchang's wife, Li Liang Zhiyang, stating that her husband, Li Bingchang, had taken the Hai Ning Steamer from Shantou to Hong Kong on January 23rd of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, and suddenly committed suicide by jumping into the sea. His luggage and three suicide notes had been forwarded by Jardine Matheson & Co. to confirm this. Therefore, she requested that the company compensate for the insured life insurance fee of

HK$50,000, etc. After receiving the letter, the Hong Kong Foreign Insurance branch forwarded it to the Foreign Insurance head office at No. 17 Bund, Shanghai for investigation. However, according to the company's articles of association, if the premium of a life insurance policyholder is paid for one year and they commit suicide, the insurance company should be liable for compensation. Therefore, the head office sent personnel to investigate whether Li Bingchang had died. On November 16th of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the head office investigated with Hua Ge, the owner of the Hai Ning Steamer, and found that there was no passenger on the Hai Ning Steamer who committed suicide by jumping into the sea and issued a certificate. Therefore, the Foreign Insurance Company had

doubts about Li Bingchang's death. During this time, Li Liang Zhiying repeatedly sent letters to the company urging them to pay the compensation. She also hired lawyer Xu Zhangguo in Guangzhou to send letters to the company, saying that if it was deliberately delayed, they would resolve it legally. The company did not pursue the matter as Li's death could not be proven, and according to the rules, the compensation would have to be paid after seven years. However, they secretly continued the investigation until recently, when they learned that Li Bingchang was indeed still alive. The previous death news was fabricated, thereby

attempting to defraud the compensation. They telegraphed Shantou, instructing Li Liang Zhiying to come to Shanghai for a face-to-face discussion. Li Liang Zhiying, along with her fellow villager Zhang Zhengde (56 years old), came to Shanghai together on the 26th of last month, staying in rooms 207 and 215 of the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road. All accommodation expenses were borne by the company. Meanwhile, Zhou Ruofu, a staff member dispatched by the Foreign Insurance Company, secretly investigated their actions. Li Liang Zhiying and Zhang Zhengde had negotiated at the head office on the 27th and 28th of last month. On the 30th, Zhou Ruofu, dispatched by the Foreign Insurance Company, suddenly saw Li Liang Zhiying going to 17

Lingnan Hostel, Wuchang Road. After Zhou investigated, it was found that Lin Yuan had checked into room 17. Lin was wearing a hair-pressing cap and looked suspicious. Fearing that it was Li Bingchang in disguise, he immediately reported to the General Police Station, which dispatched detective Haite to the Lingnan Hostel to arrest Lin Yuan. At first, he denied it, but after removing the hair-pressing cap and revealing two scars on his neck and forehead, it was confirmed that Lin Yuan was indeed Li Bingchang in disguise. He then went to the New Asia Hotel and continued to arrest Li Liang Zhiyang and Zhang Zhengde.

They were taken into custody separately.

Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunji prosecuted them for attempted fraud under Articles 339, Section 1 and 3 of the Criminal Code, and stated the above circumstances, saying that the defendant Li Bingchang admitted in the police station that he had designed the fraud due to business failure, and stated that when he took the Hai Ning Steamer, he bought a first-class ticket in a Western suit, and then changed into Chinese clothing and disembarked among the third-class passengers. After Judge Pan Zhenyang briefly interrogated the three defendants, he ordered them to be detained separately and rescheduled the trial for Friday of this week.

Discovery of Peking Man; Andersson Arrives in Shanghai 121

The Continental News reports that Dr. Andersson, who is believed to have discovered "Peking Man", quietly arrived in Shanghai on a Swedish ship a few days ago. The doctor is knowledgeable and amiable. After leaving China for nine years, he has now returned and will use Shanghai as his office, staying in the Far East for a year before returning to his hometown of Stockholm, Sweden. In accordance with the contract signed with the Geological Society of China, the doctor will discuss with his Chinese colleagues in Shanghai the publication of various papers on the discovery of antiquities in China. The doctor is currently the director of the Swedish Museum of Far Eastern Antiquities. Although he enjoys great fame, he is unwilling to enjoy his leisure in his hometown, so he has returned to China to continue his work to complete his many unfinished plans. According to reports, the doctor came to China in 1911 and served as a geological advisor to the Chinese government. In the years that followed, he engaged in the study of Chinese antiquities and related issues. His footsteps have taken him from the far north to Qinghai, and he is a frequent visitor to Henan, Shanxi, Shaanxi, and Gansu. His greatest contribution to the scientific community was the discovery of "Peking Man" in Xishan, a suburb of Beijing. The doctor has also explored the North and South Poles but still never forgets these two places.

Giant of the Stationery Industry; Wang Xiaotang Dies; Funeral Today 125

Mr. Wang Xiaotang, a native of Zhenhai, Zhejiang, lived in Shanghai for more than 40 years and was a capable and practical person who did not engage in hypocrisy. In the late Qing Dynasty, seeing that education in our country was in its infancy and undergoing reforms, and that the tools should change with the trend, he believed that if a worker wants to do a good job, he must first sharpen his tools, and that promoting cultural supplies was an urgent task. He contacted Mr. Lin Kanghou, the late Mr. Shi Liangcai, and raised funds to establish the Heji Educational Supplies Company, with Mr. Wang as the manager. He worked hard and diligently, and the business flourished, becoming well-known far and wide. Since its establishment 30 years ago, it has been the leader in the stationery industry. All those in the stationery industry in Shanghai have come from his company. He was 61 years old and still had a vibrant spirit. He wore simple clothing and was content. After the Autumn Festival, he suffered from liver disease and sought treatment from Chinese and Western doctors, but was unable to recover. He passed away at 6:00 AM on November 28th. The funeral will be held at 3:00 PM on December 3rd (today) at the China Funeral Home. It is expected that there will be a large number of people going to the Sege Road to pay their respects and look at his remains.

Amid the US Strike Wave; Canadian and Japanese Ships Arrive in Shanghai; Mail to be Sent via Siberia; Japan Plans to Add More Mail Ships 126

The Shanghai Times reports that all American ships along the Pacific coast, except for the McKinley, have completely suspended service as a result of the US shipping strike. Canadian and Japanese mail ships are benefiting greatly from this. Yesterday (1st), the Japanese Empress of the Changxing Company arrived in Shanghai, carrying a total of 900 passengers. Another Japanese ship also arrived carrying more than 200 passengers. Both ships are carrying a large amount of US mail, some of which has been delayed for a long time. The Nikkai Maru has 717 passengers going to various southern ports. The remaining hundred or so passengers are mostly well-known foreigners traveling in Shanghai, several of whom had been stranded in Honolulu for a long time. It is reported that when the ship departed from Honolulu to the Orient, it carried a total of 908 passengers. According to reports, the Japan Mail Steamship Company has made it very convenient for passengers stranded in Honolulu in the past few weeks. In accordance with US government regulations, it paid a fine of US$200 per passenger, as all foreign ships carrying passengers from one US port to another must pay this amount. However, this fee is of course borne by the passengers. Since the Nikkai Maru and the Canadian Empress departed from Hawaii and went to Canadian ports, there is no such issue. The company's staff stated yesterday that all ship tickets have been booked. Even American diplomats and military personnel going to their posts in the East have had to switch to non-American ships. The newly appointed American District Attorney for this port, Mr. Shearer, is also coming to Shanghai on a Japanese ship and is expected to arrive on the 13th of this month. It is reported that if the strike continues unabated, the Japan Mail Steamship Company plans to add more mail ships between the United States and the East to increase capacity. As for mail, the post office has agreed that if necessary, it will be shipped via Siberia, but it must be clearly marked on the envelope. The McKinley President of the Changxing Company is scheduled to set sail from Shanghai this morning, taking the route to Seattle via Japan, carrying many passengers. This is the last Pacific coast passenger and mail ship, but it is expected that it will also join the strike upon arrival in Seattle. American shipping personnel in this port now have almost nothing to do, and as the strike continues with labor and management deadlocked, it seems unlikely to be resolved anytime soon.

Yang Wendao and Ye Haisheng Appeal Case: Second Branch of the High Court Holds All-Day Trial. Yang States Judicial Independence Cannot Yield to Any Party's Intentions. Ye Says He Is Like a Lamb Subdued by a Pack of Tigers. Hong Wenwei Steps Forward to Testify, Speaking Out for Yang Wendao's Injustice. Appellants' Lawyers Subsequently List All the Suspicious Points in the Case. —Debate Adjourned Yesterday; Verdict Set for the Ninth— 130

Cantonese men Yang Wendao and Ye Haisheng (nicknamed Xiao Guangdong) were accused of premeditated murder in the case of Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo, who was shot and killed on Dith Avenue in Hongkou last winter. The police investigated and determined them to be the perpetrators. The First Special District Court filed charges against them. At the conclusion of the initial trial, Yang and Ye were both sentenced to death. However, Yang and Ye were not satisfied and each filed an appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court through their defense lawyers. The hearing was originally scheduled for the 19th of last month, but was postponed because Yang Wendao became ill in prison and was transferred to a hospital for treatment, unable to appear in court. Thus, it was postponed until

Yesterday Morning at 9 AM.

The Criminal Court President Yu Hua of the Second Branch of the High Court, along with Judges Zhou and Nie, specially convened a collegiate bench, ordering Yang and Ye to be brought forward and summoning witnesses for questioning. Security was tight inside and outside the courtroom. Prosecutor Lin Wopeng also attended to perform his duties. The appellants' attorneys, Zhang Zhirang, Guo Qiming, etc., and the police attorney Ru Baoyi, all appeared in court. After Judge Yu questioned Yang and Ye about their ages and origins, he immediately ordered them to state their reasons for appeal. First, Yang Wendao detailed the reasons for his appeal and the process by which he was framed by Yang Jianzhong, stating that he knew nothing about the case of the murdered Japanese sailor and, having

No Grudge

Against the Japanese sailor, why would he kill this unrelated person? Everyone has a patriotic heart, but killing a Japanese soldier would be of no benefit. Someone named Yang Guimei came to tell me that the police were going to arrest me. I did not heed her words because I had never broken the law. Yang then left in a hurry. Later, Luo Wende came to inform me that Yang Jianzhong had already reported it to the police, so the police were going to arrest me. I still did not listen and on the 16th, I looked for Yang Jianzhong at the Hubei Small Native Place Association and met Yang Chujie. At that time, Yang Guimei was also at the entrance of the association. I then slapped her cheek, blaming her for

Not Speaking Recklessly,

Acknowledging that she had been fooled by Yang Jianzhong. After that, someone followed me all day. As a result, two plainclothes Japanese men took me and Chen Yongsheng into a car and drove us to the police station. The Western inspector held a book in his hand. I immediately admitted that the book was used to hide guns in the past, but it had not been used for a long time. If I were involved in the case, why wouldn't I have fled and instead kept the evidence? The next day, I was taken to court for interrogation. I still admitted that the book was used to hide guns, but seeing that the gun placed in the book's hole did not match, I was very surprised. From then on, I denied that the book was my original book. This book's

Method of Cutting a Hole

Was taught by Yang Jianzhong. In February of this year, Yang came to my house. My child was holding the book and playing with it. I went upstairs because of something. When I came downstairs, Yang Jianzhong had left and the book my child was holding was also gone. From this, it can be seen that Yang Jianzhong must have planted the evidence to frame me. In short, Yang and his cohort were acting according to a deliberate plan. Thus, at the preliminary hearing, Investigator Zhang was brought to testify and he testified that he saw white paper shaped like a handgun at Zheng Huimin's house, and the letters "PB" were written on the paper. In addition to creating this book, they also forged a letter, stamped with the

"Benevolence Association"

Seal and my personal seal. All the items seized from my house were presented at the preliminary hearing, but this letter was not presented. In fact, this letter and the book are both related. I request the court to order the police to also present the letter for research. Now I have appealed to your court because I harbor an unjust grievance. If the book really belonged to me, then there would be no fingerprints on the book. Now, the preliminary hearing sentenced me to death based solely on this one book. Although I am not familiar with the law, I believe the law would never be so simple. The preliminary hearing witness accused me of gambling and etc. with Koreans at the Benevolence Association, but the association's second landlord and tea boy have both testified that

This Never Happened.

Regarding what was involved, only Ye Haisheng confessed that I wanted to expand the Hongkou sphere of influence, so I had the Japanese killed. If I really had the Japanese killed, I could have discarded the murder weapon, so why not discard the book used to hide the gun? Ye also confessed that I gave him the gun on the way, so why didn't I give him the book as well? If I did indeed give the gun to Ye, then please ask if there are any of my fingerprints on the gun. Central Bank Inspection Report. 133

Central Bank Exchange Note Issuance Reserve 311th Inspection Report states that the Association is responsible for inspecting the Bank's exchange note issuance amount and reserve fund in accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law. The 311th inspection was held at the Bank's Issuance Bureau on November 28, 25th year of the Republic of China, and the inspection results are reported as follows: A. Total Exchange Note Issuance: Silver dollars 31,294,147.77 yuan, including silver dollar notes 27,533,847.72 yuan and fractional currency notes 3,760,300.05 yuan. Total Exchange Note Reserve Fund: 31,294,147.77 yuan, including cash reserve silver dollars 20,456,717.77 yuan. This cash reserve includes 92,434,577.48 yuan deposited in the Bank's issuing general and branch treasuries and various branches, 112,132,599.52 yuan deposited with other banks, and a guarantee reserve equivalent to 108,374,300 yuan in silver dollars. B. Total Issuance of Customs Gold Exchange Notes: 400,963.07 yuan in Customs Gold. Total Customs Gold Exchange Note Reserve Fund: 400,963.07 yuan in Customs Gold. This reserve fund includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, with a fixed price of 51.68 Customs Gold, totaling 400,963.07 yuan in Customs Gold. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve shall be at least 60%, and the remainder shall be a guarantee reserve of legal collateral. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This report is hereby made. November 30, 25th year of the Republic of China. Central Bank Supervisory Committee Chairman Li Fuxun, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilong.

Although Li Zhenzhong was Invited to Help, the Xin Team Still Lost to Xintong - 29 to 41 139

The first game of the current West Youth Basketball Tournament last night was declared sold out because Li Zhenzhong was invited from Beijing to Shanghai to help the Xin team defeat the Xintong Sea Robber team. There was almost no standing room in the West Youth Gymnasium. However, the result of the game was that the Xin team ultimately failed to crush the Sea Robber's edge and, with a score of 29 to 41, still allowed the Sea Robber to maintain its undefeated reputation in the league. The score at halftime was 15 to 10, with Xintong also leading. In another game, the Mai team defeated Qingguang by a large margin, with a score of 65 to 30.

Lack of Cooperation

The Xin team's defeat, in a nutshell, was due to the team's lack of coordination. The participation of Li Zhenzhong and Xu Zhaoxiong made it even more difficult for the team to cooperate. Although it was a good strategy for Li Zhenzhong to switch to defense to monitor the tall Lan Yin's shooting, it did not have a significant effect. The accurate shooting of Shi Guiya and Peisel and the ingenious tactics of Carson and others ultimately forced the Xin team, which was like a heap of loose sand, to concede defeat. Xintong's familiarity with pure teamwork was no accident. Feng Nianhua's performance was the best on the Xin team. Li Zhenzhong could not accomplish anything alone, and Xu Zhaoxiong was of no use.

Seven Points Behind

At the start of the game, the Xin team had Feng Nianhua and Li Zhenzhong as left and right forwards, Chen Xianglong in the center, and Sun Baoqing and Lu Zhongen as guards. Later, due to the pressure in the backcourt, when the score was 7 to 11, Xu Zhaoxiong entered the game to take Li's position, and Xianglong was taken off the court. The situation was very tense, but the Xin team ultimately had no hope of advancing, and the score difference remained at six or seven points. The halftime score was 15 to 10.

Impossible to Save

At the start of the second half, after some initial resistance, Feng Nianhua scored twice, bringing the score to 16 to 19, which seemed promising. It was also the closest the overall score came. However, Shi Guiya, Lamb, and Jin scored six consecutive points, bringing the score to 16 to 25. The Xin team was in danger again. After 22 to 29, Chen Xianglong entered the game and Xu Zhaoxiong was taken off again, but the situation did not improve. The Xin team's defense occasionally made mistakes, and Peisel and Lan Yin scored one after another. Shi Guiya scored three goals in an instant, and the score jumped to 39 to 23. The Xin team suffered a major blow, and although they struggled to the utmost, they were at the end of their rope. The outcome was thus determined, and the final result was 29 to 41 in favor of Xintong.

Education News

Jiangsu Province County Elementary Schools - Teacher Salary Standards - Approved by the Education Department and Filed with the Ministry of Education 148

The Jiangsu Province Education Department has approved the salary standards for principals and teachers of county elementary schools in Jiangsu Province and filed them with the Ministry of Education. The following are the details of this method: (1) The Jiangsu Province Education Department has formulated this method in order to implement the Ministry's order to increase the salaries of elementary school teachers and adjust the salary standards of principals and teachers of elementary schools in various counties, and to improve educational efficiency. (2) The qualifications of elementary school principals and teachers are divided into the following five levels: (Level A) Graduates of normal universities, university education colleges, education departments, higher normal schools, and vocational normal schools. (Level B) Graduates of old-system normal schools, senior high school normal departments, and special normal departments. (Level C) Graduates of provincial rural normal schools and those who have not passed the examination and verification. (Level D) Graduates of provincial and county teacher training classes and those who have passed the examination and verification. (Level E) Those who meet the qualifications of substitute teachers in elementary school regulations. (3) The monthly salary of elementary school teachers must be determined according to the aforementioned qualifications and grades, with a difference of 2 to 4 yuan between each grade. However, the starting salary for each grade must be in accordance with the following regulations: (Level A qualification) starting salary of at least 20 yuan; (Level B qualification) starting salary of at least 18 yuan; (Level C qualification) starting salary of at least 16 yuan; (Level D qualification) starting salary of at least 14 yuan; (Level E qualification) starting salary of at least 12 yuan. (4) Elementary school principals in junior primary schools will be promoted by one grade; those with three grades will be promoted by one and a half grades, and so on. (5) Full-time teachers in senior primary schools will be promoted to the starting salary; those who concurrently serve as principals of elementary schools with two grades will be promoted by one grade, those with four grades will be promoted by three grades, and so on. (6) Junior primary schools shall have one teacher per grade. For grades with an average of 40 children or more, one subject teacher may be added. Teachers who teach all subjects in a grade may be promoted one grade for every seven children exceeding 35 children. Teachers who teach three grades may be promoted one grade for every ten children exceeding 40 children, but the maximum number of children per grade is limited to 60. (7) Senior primary schools shall have two full-time teachers and one subject teacher per two grades. For each grade with 40 or more children, the full-time teacher may be promoted by half a grade, and for every five children over 40, they shall be promoted once in proportion. If a school has only senior grades or only one grade, it shall be calculated accordingly. (8) If the actual number of children in each grade of a senior primary school is less than 30, the full-time teacher will be demoted by one grade; if the salary is less than 25, the school will be suspended or merged. If the actual number of children in each grade of a junior primary school is less than 25, the full-time teacher will be demoted by one grade; if the salary is less than 30, the school will be suspended or merged. (9) Teachers who have been promoted due to an increase in the number of children may be demoted at any time in accordance with the reduced number of children if the number of children decreases. (10) The number of children stipulated in the above articles may be increased or decreased by the counties in accordance with local conditions, subject to approval by the Education Department. (11) Principals and teachers who work hard and have excellent performance, and have been commended or praised by provincial and county supervisors, may be promoted by one or two grades. Those who continue to strive for excellence after promotion may be promoted again, but those who are declining in performance may be demoted at any time. (12) Staff who have already been given additional labor remuneration in various counties may be promoted by several grades as appropriate to maintain their original treatment, but thereafter they may be promoted or demoted at any time in accordance with the provisions of the preceding article. (13) Each school should submit the resumes and supporting documents of the teachers it intends to hire to the Education Bureau or the first department of the county government for verification of the starting salary grade within one month before the start of each semester. If the qualifications are not met, the department may order the school to hire another teacher or directly appoint one. (14) Each department shall conduct a teacher registration decision within two months before the start of each semester. When teachers with qualifications in the four categories of A, B, C, and D who have been registered cannot be fully employed, teachers with qualifications in category E may not be employed. (15) The number of students in each grade shall be calculated on the average of the number of people inspected by the supervisors and education committees, but pre-school children under the age of six and after-school students who have reached the age limit must be uniformly excluded. (16) The funding standards for schools at all levels, which were originally calculated on the basis of grades or have no fixed salary grade and lack the conditions stipulated in this method, should be re-established according to the minimum requirements outlined and forwarded to the authorities for approval. Standards that have been originally established and the corresponding budget exceeded what has been set in this new method need to have the starting salary grade raised. Those budgets that do not meet this minimum requirement need to have funds allocated to fill in that difference. (17) This method shall be promulgated and implemented by the Provincial Government Committee.

Overview of Shanghai Municipal Council Elementary Schools (5) 156

— Special Report by This Newspaper, Investigation by Hu Zuyin

12. Medical Facilities

Medical services for students in the Municipal Council's elementary schools are provided by the School Medical Office established by the Municipal Council's Health Department. The School Medical Office was established in December of the 20th year and operates under the guidance of the Director of the Health Department. It assists the Education Department in providing medical care for students in all Chinese elementary schools. The Health Department employs one Western school medical officer, two Chinese school medical officers, and five Chinese school nurses with specialized training and experience, who are responsible for examining the physical condition of children in various elementary schools, as well as detecting, preventing, and treating some of the students' illnesses.

According to the School Medical Report for the 24th year, a total of 1,967 students from four elementary schools were examined throughout the year, including 1,351 boys and 616 girls. As a result of the school medical officers' examination of the physical condition of 1,967 students, the following deficiencies were discovered:

Suffering from Trachoma: 1,113 students

Suffering from Infectious Skin Diseases: 442 students

Suffering from Heart Defects: 864 students

Suffering from Lung Defects: 395 students

Suffering from Tonsil Defects: 1,252 students

Suffering from Visual Defects: 89 students

Suffering from Ascariasis: 188 students

Suffering from Other Diseases: 78 students

After examining the children's physical condition, the school medical officers handle the cases in three ways: (1) For children whose physical condition is satisfactory in all aspects, the Medical Office informs their parents that the student can continue to attend school as usual; (2) For children who have some deficiencies in their physical condition, but are not contagious or do not affect other students, the Medical Office informs their parents to seek medical treatment, but the student can still attend school as usual; (3) For children who suffer from infectious diseases that are likely to affect the health of other children, the Medical Office informs their parents to seek immediate medical treatment, and the student is not allowed to attend school. Due to insufficient funds and equipment, the School Medical Office is temporarily unable to treat common illnesses in children.

When children arrive at school each day, the class teacher checks them over every morning. Children who are ill or suspected of being ill are sent by the class teacher to the principal's office and then to the school medical officer for examination. If the medical officer confirms that the student is ill, the student is sent back home and their parents are asked to seek immediate medical treatment. If the student suffers from an infectious disease, they must be isolated for a certain period before returning to school. The relevant classrooms in the school will be disinfected immediately to prevent the spread of infection. The length of the isolation period depends on the nature of the infectious disease. After a sick student recovers, they must first go to the School Medical Office for examination. Only after the medical officer proves that the student has recovered and issues a certificate of recovery can the student return to school with the certificate. In total, the number of sick students in all schools in the 24th year was 1,084; of these, 562 dropped out due to illness, and 522 recovered and returned to school.

Cotton Yarn Prices Fluctuate Greatly; Rising and Falling Suddenly; It Can Only Be Called Speculation; As a Result, Prices Rose Again by 1.2.3.4 Yuan Compared to the Previous Day; The Equivalent in Silver Taels Has Reached 192 Taels, Exceeding the Price of Third-Grade Yarn by More Than Ten Yuan 157

The cotton yarn market is unpredictable, and the situation is as chaotic as hemp. The bulls and bears are both strong. In the early morning, general floating traders had overnight market buy orders. At the opening, the rising trend was sharp, jumping up three or four yuan. Subsequently, profit-taking led to a sharp and tragic fall. The opening in the afternoon was still flat, but after one round, it started to jump up. This month, a high of 260 yuan was discovered, plus the consolidated tax of 8.58 yuan (equivalent to more than 192 taels in the old standard), which has exceeded the high price of the past five years. As for the spot yarn transactions, they have turned sluggish due to the high price. The Shanghai futures yarn price is more than ten yuan higher than the Osaka third-grade yarn. In fact, both parties are trading, and there are too many chips. The bulls are pushing up the price and squeezing the shorts too much, so the market is showing signs of a collapse.

Rising and Falling, Falling and Rising

In the morning opening of the labeled yarn market, due to the previous day's limit up, panic among investors reached its peak. General retail investors were eager to cover their positions, and the market situation was unusually mixed. The December contract surged 4.2 yuan, the December-January contract rose 3.9 yuan to 2 yuan, and the March contract rose only 0.5 yuan. Unexpectedly, at the second round of trading, the Osaka third-grade yarn was calm, and the intermediate term fell by 78 cents. Moreover, the rising trend was too violent, causing a large number of profit-takers to exit the market. At the same time, spot yarn transactions were stagnant due to the high price. The market situation turned sharply downwards, with the December contract falling by 4 yuan and the December-January contract falling tragically by 6.3 yuan to 63 yuan. The closing market was flat, and as a result, the prices of each month were all down from 8 cents to 1.5 yuan and 2.2 yuan compared to the closing price of the previous day. At the afternoon opening, the near-term contracts were firm and did not move, while the far-term contracts rose by 1 yuan. At the second round, the December contract's rising trend resumed, jumping up 2.9 yuan, and the January contract jumped up by 4 yuan. At the third round, the rising trend became more intense, with the December contract rising to 60 yuan, and the January contract rising by another 4.5 yuan. The far contracts closed up 2.5 yuan. Some profit-takers sold off, causing a retracement of 1.5 yuan to 3.2 yuan. As a result, each month rose by 4.1 yuan to 5.5 yuan compared to the morning close. It was found that Gengfeng sold 6,450 bales, Dafu 1,350 bales, Deda 2,350 bales, Chengji 3,050 bales, Yuda 4,600 bales, Daji 1,350 bales, Mingde 2,100 bales, Shenchang 1,350 bales, Changyu 1,700 bales, Renfeng 2,700 bales, Yuan Yi 1,550 bales, Hengchang 1,050 bales, Tonghe 6,800 bales, Dafeng 7,400 bales, Xincheng 3,000 bales, and Jinchang 1,850 bales. The cotton market is falling sharply, which is inversely proportional to the yarn market. There Is Demand for American Cotton in Both Near and Distant Months 159

Spot cotton was firm, and the cloth market was more expensive. Later, the bulls liquidated, and the rising trend slowed down. At the close, public buying saw a rebound. Spot cotton rose 15 points, and futures rose 8 to 16 points. British spot cotton was unchanged, and futures rose 45 points. Indian cotton exporters bought in large quantities, and brokers sold off Pingguol and Aomura, while speculators sold off Bairuo Creek. Piece Goods; Cotton Cloth Rising Trend Becoming More Intense; Heavyweight White Twill Flannel Rising by 56 Cents; Prices in Various Places Also Rising Sharply Due to the Influence of the Shanghai Market 163

Yesterday, the cotton cloth market situation, with the unprecedented rise in yarn prices yesterday and today, was exciting, reaching its peak, and the rising trend of piece goods became more and more intense. The selling prices changed rapidly. Compared with the market on the previous day, white cloth, fine twill, raw cloth, grey cloth, and coarse cloth jumped (per piece) by 1.2 cents. Blue cloth, shirting, printed flannel, and woolen cloth rose (per piece) by 1.2.3 cents. Spot goods in the market were in great shortage, and customers had difficulty getting goods and were in urgent need, so they offered high prices to buy them. For example, the small amount of heavyweight white twill flannel sold at a price that jumped (per piece) by 5.6 cents. Only printed drill, serge, crepe de chine, and colored drill goods were weak in sales due to seasonal reasons. Although the price of grey cloth continued to rise, the recent market has seen a fall (per piece) of 2 cents. Although the shirting selling price was slightly firm, sales were still sluggish. However, blue cloth and colored twill were in increased demand from customers, and there was a shortage of supply of grey cloth, so the market followed the fine cloth and fine twill, advancing steadily. Local sales markets of various customer guilds were excited by the rise in the Shanghai market, and the upward trend was also rapid, so the market price rose more quickly.

Grain; Flour Futures Rise and Fall Irregularly; A Big Rise Followed by a Small Retracement Is Also Natural 164

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices of each month showed a trend of rising first and then retracing to the previous level. At the beginning of the opening, due to the Chicago quotation, the near-term rose by 1.0 yuan and the far-term rose by 0.5 to 0.1 yuan, etc. Canadian flour rose by 45 cents, so after the opening, the current month once rose to 4.025 yuan, which was 4 cents higher than the previous day. The rising momentum of the months below January was also strong, and trading was very active. The April contract alone rose by 6 cents. Then, a large number of profitable bulls withdrew, and the factories also sold new chips, so the market gradually fell, down 34 cents from the highest point. By the afternoon opening, the prices of flowers and yarn rose but fell back, people's hearts were again empty, and the factories continued to sell, so the near-term and far-term contracts fell by 34 cents. In the last few rounds, the current month to February fell by 23 cents compared to the previous day, and MarchApril was still 1 cent better. This kind of irregular rise and fall situation seems to be speculation in heat again.

Wheat Prices Continue to Rise and Then Fall Back 165

Yesterday's wheat futures market, after the opening in the morning, the prices of each month showed a stable start followed by a very fierce reversal. At the beginning of the opening, due to the quotation of foreign wheat, it continued to rise by 1.0 yuan, followed by a rise of 1 cent to 45 cents. Therefore, the market was very firm, and the opening prices of each month were better by 12 cents to 34 cents. However, because the market value was too high, the buyers were unable to raise the prices at will. When it came to the opening in the afternoon, because the flour market fell back, the general profit-taking bulls also withdrew one after another, causing the selling to be smooth and the market to fall sharply by 678 cents. After that, the situation could not be measured by common sense due to the unpredictable changes in the situation. In the current wheat market, customers sold back and the price was called up by another 1.5 cents, and Fufeng opened 6,000 bags, eating up to 6.35 yuan at the highest price, followed by 1.5 cents.

The Problem That Ordinary Rice Is Facing Is Having No Outlet 166

Yesterday's ordinary rice market situation remained flat and soft. Although the outgoing of local rice was active, the supply was greater than the demand, and the market continued to be weak. Recently, the source has been 10,000 to tens of thousands of bags per day, while the digestion is only 34,000 to 67,000 bags. The Guangdong guild, which used to be a major outlet, has been silent for a long time, which is the main reason for the weakness of the market. Although there was some embellishment yesterday, it was ultimately too slight to cause people's hearts to go up. Moreover, when the inter-provincial transportation was implemented, and the prices of yarn, flowers, flour, wheat, oil, and beans in the Shanghai market soared, it caused the production area dealers to transport as much as possible, leading to a slump. If sales to Guangdong and North China were to be smooth again, the market price would recover quickly. Because rice is the main food for the people, most people in the industry are optimistic about it. The whole day's openings included 4,300 bags of Jiangxi rice, 1,640 bags of Ningbo and Wenzhou rice, and 200 bags of Jiangbei rice, and the prices were similar to those of the previous market.

The Arrival of Rice at Hexia Turned Decadent; Some Rice Boats Were Detained and Not Allowed to Pass 167

(North Shanghai) It was recently heard from the interior that the export of steamed buns was quite prosperous, so the neighboring counties blocked rice boats from crossing the border to Shanghai in the Jiwang Temple section the night before for the sake of the people's food. There are currently forty to fifty rice boats being detained. Yesterday morning, customers came to report to the Rice Industry Association, and the executive members Fu and Jiang went to request the county government to dredge and release the rice to Shanghai. It will not be clear until the day after tomorrow. Yesterday, the arrival of goods at Hexia was scarce, and the price of white rice increased by several cents to one cent. Bo Dao's sales to customers were quite good, and the price increased by seven or eight cents. The price of Yang Du Bu Ke Jian also increased by one cent. The prices of all other goods increased by nearly one cent.

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, a total of one hundred companies arrived from various guilds, with a total of 21,200 shi of goods, half of which was thick and thin japonica rice. The reception of Bo Dao rice was still relatively active, with more than 6,000 bags from Tianjin, Yantai, and Qingdao guilds, so the initial market was quite tight, and the market price rose by five cents. However, later, due to the relationship between identifying the quality of rice and the accuracy of samples, the buyers and sellers were again in a situation of disagreement, and there was no definite way until about 5 pm, so they dispersed without results, causing the prices of Bo Dao rice from various guilds to fail to open. The sales of thick japonica rice to urban and rural shops and customers have improved slightly, and the customer guilds have also sold 1,200 to 1,300 bags, so the market price has recovered by a few cents. The situation of Du Jian rice is similar, only Yang Jian rice has not seen ups and downs due to the high price. Yin Yuanhua is in a stable situation due to the scarcity of the source.

Miscellaneous Jiangxi Specialty: A Large Shipment of Nanfeng Honey Tangerines Arrives in Shanghai 171

Nanfeng honey tangerines are small in size with thin skin, few seeds, no residue, and a taste as sweet as honey, hence the name "honey tangerine." They have a fragrant aroma that lasts for a long time, and can moisten the lungs, quench thirst, regulate qi, resolve phlegm, generate fluids, and treat coughs. The peel and the fibrous strands can both be used as medicinal ingredients, and have the effect of dispelling cold and wind. They are the best choice for fruit baskets and a giant amongst tangerines. However, due to limited production and inconvenient transportation, this renowned product, famous throughout the country, has not been able to reach major cities. As a result, they were previously tribute items, and few common people had the opportunity to taste them. The Jiangxi Provincial Rural Cooperative Business Committee has organized tangerine farmers to promote cooperative sales, hoping to facilitate the flow of goods. Moreover, the selling price is not high, which is good news for gentlemen in Shanghai who like to eat tangerines. It is reported that the four major companies on Nanjing Road and Guanshengyuan China National Products Company are acting as sales agents.

Metals: Prices of Metals Rise Together Domestically and Abroad 172

Recently, the metal market has been very good. Overseas telegrams frequently report increases. For example, bamboo steel bars have risen to six pounds and nine shillings, sixteen shillings better than before. New iron products (such as foreign coin sheets, angle iron, and square iron) have also risen to six pounds and five shillings, a more robust ten shillings or so higher than before. Although transactions have not been seen, people's confidence and market sentiment have expanded extraordinarily. Therefore, the market prices of steel bars and new iron products in this port have also increased by several jiao to several yuan. English steel plates are sold in this port at twelve or thirteen yuan for two and a half li, ten yuan for half a fen, nine yuan and five jiao for seven and a half li, and eight yuan and seven or eight jiao for one fen. Overseas market prices have also increased by one or two pounds. It is said that transactions in seven and a half li are particularly strong. It is reported that three to four thousand dan were opened yesterday and handled by the Qingdao gang.

Silk and Tea: Tsatlee Silk Remains Popular and Strong, Rising Ten Yuan Over Last Week 173

Yesterday, the Yokohama silk market sharply declined. Spot prices plummeted by thirty-five yuan, and futures fell sharply by thirty-nine yuan. New York also followed with a sharp drop. Standard silk for both near and distant terms fell by five and a half to six cents, equivalent to a drop of about twenty-six yuan and six jiao in the Shanghai market. Prices for all raw silk items in New York were uniformly down by a little over two cents. The Lyon silk market felt quite numb. Except for Wentung silk, which rose by one franc due to the previous day's New York rebound, all other silk products opened at the original price. The Shanghai silk market was even more depressed. A telegram from New York indicated a purchase limit of 750 yuan for White Factory B grade. Details of the transaction are currently unknown. Indochina Tsatlee silk and other types remained popular and strong, selling at 605 yuan in the afternoon, a strong rise of [ten] yuan over last week. Therefore, domestic silk merchants and hoarders are even more eager to hoard goods, but judging from the overseas silk market, it does not seem to be so optimistic.

Chinese Silk May Have No Foothold in the U.S., Squeezed by Japanese Silk and Pushed Aside by Italian Silk 174

According to a report released by the Silk Association of America on New York's raw silk inventory, sales, and imports for November, business was quite good for raw silk in New York this month. The total amount of raw silk imported was 50,814 bales, an increase of 6,974 bales compared to last month and 9,121 bales compared to the same month last year. The total consumption was 40,401 bales, a decrease of 2,692 bales compared to last month, but an increase of 2,389 bales compared to the same month last year. The total ending inventory was 10,713 bales, an increase of 10,413 bales compared to last month, but a decrease of 1,403 bales compared to the same month last year. Looking at the evolution of the various figures, it is not difficult to infer the current trend of the silk market. Furthermore, although Shanghai silk exports to the United States increased by 480 bales in November compared to October, they decreased by about 1,400 bales compared to last year. In terms of consumption, the amount in November decreased by 183 bales compared to the previous month and 1,332 bales compared to the same month last year. The total ending inventory was 2,066 bales, an increase of 336 bales compared to last month and a decrease of 2,795 bales compared to the same month last year. Looking at these statistics, the decrease in the ending inventory is a good phenomenon, but the significant decline in imports and consumption is cause for concern. At the same time, the sudden rise of European silk exports to the United States is evident when comparing this year's figures with last year's. Regardless of imports or consumption, the increase in these figures gradually surpasses that of Shanghai silk. Therefore, the export of Chinese silk is not only squeezed by Japanese silk but also pushed aside by Italian silk. Even if the European and American silk markets can be better, it is still difficult to be very optimistic about the sale of our Chinese silk. Moreover, the Shanghai silk market often feels like there are accounts but no goods, or goods that are difficult to sell. The November New York raw silk statistics, along with figures from the previous month and the same month last year, are listed below for comparison.
